[[Source]](https://starwars.fandom.com/wiki/Template:Character)

:   "*Remember that war is like a fire across the galaxy. It spreads and it consumes. We must never waver in the face of that fire. We are keepers of the peace. We are Jedi. The Republic needs us more than ever, which means our faith in the Force, our connection to the Force must never waver.*"
:   ―Mace Windu[[13]](#cite_note-Brotherhood-13)

**Mace Windu** was a revered [Force-sensitive](/wiki/Force-sensitive "Force-sensitive") [human](/wiki/Human "Human") [male](/wiki/Gender "Gender") [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") and member of the [Jedi High Council](/wiki/Jedi_High_Council "Jedi High Council") during the last [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") of the [Republic Era](/wiki/Republic_Era "Republic Era"). During his [time](/wiki/Time "Time") in the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order"), he once served as [an elected leader](/wiki/Master_of_the_Order "Master of the Order") of the [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi") and, during the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars"), as a [Jedi General](/wiki/Jedi_General "Jedi General") in The [Grand Army of the Republic](/wiki/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic "Grand Army of the Republic"). He was the greatest champion of The Jedi Order and promoted its ancient traditions amidst the growing influence of the [dark side of the Force](/wiki/Dark_side_of_the_Force "Dark side of the Force") in the [corrupt, declining days of the Republic](/wiki/Republic_Era "Republic Era").

During a [mission to Metagos](/wiki/Mission_to_Metagos "Mission to Metagos"), Windu went by the pseudonym **Solver**. When the [Separatist Crisis](/wiki/Separatist_Crisis "Separatist Crisis") spawned the birth of the [Confederacy of Independent Systems](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems "Confederacy of Independent Systems") and [sparked](/wiki/First_Battle_of_Geonosis "First Battle of Geonosis") the [Clone](/wiki/Cloning "Cloning") Wars, Windu and the Jedi rallied to the defense of the Republic and became the leaders of the Grand [Army](/wiki/Army "Army") of the Republic. Throughout the war, Windu served the Jedi and the Republic in various capacities—on the battlefield in command of the [clone army](/wiki/Clone_trooper "Clone trooper"), on [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant") as an overseer of the war effort and an [advisor](/wiki/Advisor "Advisor") to [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor") [Sheev Palpatine](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious"), and even as a [diplomat](/wiki/Diplomat "Diplomat") to contested [worlds](/wiki/Planet "Planet"), despite his disdain of [politics](/wiki/Politics "Politics"). His exploits on the frontline served as a reminder of his reputation as a renowned Jedi warrior.

As the war drew to a close, Windu became increasingly suspicious of the chancellor's motives, as Palpatine had amassed near-dictatorial control over the [Galactic Senate](/wiki/Galactic_Senate "Galactic Senate"), and sensed the rising power of the dark side in [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy"). His suspicions were confirmed when [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker"), a [Jedi Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight") and the [Chosen One](/wiki/Chosen_One "Chosen One") of ancient prophecy, discovered that Palpatine was [Darth](/wiki/Darth "Darth") Sidious, the [Dark Lord of the Sith](/wiki/Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith "Dark Lord of the Sith") who manipulated and deceived the Republic and the Separatist Alliance into war. Windu, along with Jedi Masters [Kit Fisto](/wiki/Kit_Fisto "Kit Fisto"), [Saesee Tiin](/wiki/Saesee_Tiin "Saesee Tiin"), and [Agen Kolar](/wiki/Agen_Kolar "Agen Kolar"), [confronted](/wiki/Duel_in_Palpatine%27s_office "Duel in Palpatine's office") Palpatine with the intention of [arresting](/wiki/Prison "Prison") him. Instead, the Dark [Lord](/wiki/Lord "Lord") attacked them, striking them down one by one until only Windu was left. Windu bested Palpatine in the confrontation and—deciding the chancellor was too dangerous to be left alive due to his influence over the government—prepared to strike him down, but Anakin Skywalker intervened and allowed the Sith Lord to kill Windu. Skywalker had fallen to the temptation of the dark side and became known as Darth Vader.

Windu's actions led Palpatine to brand the Jedi as traitors to the Republic. The chancellor executed [Order 66](/wiki/Order_66 "Order 66"), [forcing the clone troopers across the galaxy to turn against and kill their Jedi leaders](/wiki/Behavioral_modification_biochip "Behavioral modification biochip"), marking the [fall](/wiki/Great_Jedi_Purge "Great Jedi Purge") of the Jedi Order [and separatists](/wiki/Mission_to_Mustafar "Mission to Mustafar"). Palpatine [transformed](/wiki/Proclamation_of_the_New_Order "Proclamation of the New Order") the Republic into the [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire") and the [Emperor's](/wiki/Galactic_Emperor "Galactic Emperor") [new regime](/wiki/New_Order "New Order") promoted [anti-Jedi sentiment](/wiki/Anti-Jedi_sentiment "Anti-Jedi sentiment") across the galaxy. Through [propaganda](/wiki/Propaganda "Propaganda"), the Empire portrayed Windu as the leader of a [criminal gang](/wiki/Jedi_assault_team "Jedi assault team") of Jedi who caused the outbreak of the Clone Wars. In spite of the propaganda, some of Windu's actions were remembered with fondness; [General](/wiki/General "General") [Cham Syndulla](/wiki/Cham_Syndulla "Cham Syndulla"), who served alongside Windu during the [Battle of Ryloth](/wiki/Battle_of_Ryloth "Battle of Ryloth"), remembered Windu with great respect and told the tale of how Windu helped him liberate [Ryloth](/wiki/Ryloth "Ryloth") in a battle that earned Windu the name "**The Hammer of Ryloth**."

## Biography

### Early life

#### Jedi youngling

:   "*I'm never going to be able to build my* lightsaber*.*"  
    "*Patience, young Mace. The secret is that the pieces never needed to be* built*.*"
:   ―Mace Windu and Huyang[[14]](#cite_note-Age_of_Republic-14)

 [![Professor Huyang assisted young Mace Windu with building his lightsaber.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/12/HuyangWindu-TheWeapon.png/revision/latest?cb=20241113171643) [![Professor Huyang assisted young Mace Windu with building his lightsaber.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/12/HuyangWindu-TheWeapon.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/205?cb=20241113171643)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/12/HuyangWindu-TheWeapon.png/revision/latest?cb=20241113171643) 

Professor Huyang assisted young Mace Windu with building his lightsaber.

 

Mace Windu was [born](/wiki/Reproduction "Reproduction") on the [planet](/wiki/Planet "Planet") [Haruun Kal](/wiki/Haruun_Kal "Haruun Kal")[[1]](#cite_note-SWJB-1) in the [year](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") [72 BBY](/wiki/72_BBY "72 BBY")[[2]](#cite_note-Birth_date-2) as a child of the most powerful members of his tribe.[[8]](#cite_note-Glass_Abyss-8) Like most other [toddlers](/wiki/Youngling "Youngling") from Haruun Kal, Windu received an inoculation that left a small scar on his body.[[15]](#cite_note-Windu2-15) As an infant, he took a liking to the lushfruit, a [violet](/wiki/Color "Color") fruit in which the associated color would subconsciously become his favorite.[[8]](#cite_note-Glass_Abyss-8)

A year after his birth, his [parents](/wiki/Parent "Parent") were ambushed by [garu-bears](/wiki/Garu-bear "Garu-bear") and his mother placed him in a high [tree](/wiki/Tree "Tree") for safety. Both parents were [killed](/wiki/Death "Death") in the ensuring conflict but Mace was rescued by other warriors nearby, noted for his lack of grief from having unintentionally tapped into the Force, resulting in him being unusually calm. Although the warrior were unaware of why, they found the ordeal odd. Orphaned, the tribe is later visited by a Jedi whom happened upon Windu after hearing of his parent's brutal end and "strangeness" from the tribe, concluding possible force sensitivity. His tribe invokes a ancient ritual of choosing to decide his fate which included a lushfruit, a puzzle pyramid, and the shell of a lightsaber. Windu ultimately chose the lightsaber shell.[[8]](#cite_note-Glass_Abyss-8)

Due to his [natural affinity of the Force](/wiki/Force-sensitive "Force-sensitive") and with his tribe's support, Windu was sent to the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order")[[8]](#cite_note-Glass_Abyss-8)[[5]](#cite_note-SWE-5)—a monastic order of protectors, sworn to defend the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic"), and known as the guardians of peace and justice in [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy")[[16]](#cite_note-DatabankJO-16)—to learn the [Jedi arts](/wiki/Jedi_training "Jedi training").[[6]](#cite_note-JoRMW4-6) Windu never responded well to [Grand Master](/wiki/Grand_Master "Grand Master") [Yoda](/wiki/Yoda "Yoda")'s sense of humor. As a youngling, he was taught to "let go" and trust in the Force.[[17]](#cite_note-Queen's_Peril-17) He also came to believe he was abandoned by his parents.[[8]](#cite_note-Glass_Abyss-8)

As a [Jedi youngling](/wiki/Jedi_Initiate "Jedi Initiate"), Windu endeavored to create [his own](/wiki/Mace_Windu%27s_lightsaber "Mace Windu's lightsaber") [lightsaber](/wiki/Lightsaber "Lightsaber") after obtaining an [amethyst](/wiki/Color "Color")-colored [kyber crystal](/wiki/Kyber_crystal "Kyber crystal"). He initially failed in the effort, however, causing Windu to doubt his ability to pass this particular rite in [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi") training. After observing Windu's struggle, [Professor](/wiki/Professor "Professor") [Huyang](/wiki/Huyang "Huyang") concluded that the youngling had neither the patience nor the correct understanding to complete his lightsaber. The [droid](/wiki/Droid "Droid") instructor advised Windu to temper his emotions. The secret, according to Huyang, was that a lightsaber's components never needed to be "built."[[14]](#cite_note-Age_of_Republic-14) One of Windu's instructors was [T'ra Saa](/wiki/T%27ra_Saa "T'ra Saa"), whom the young Windu sparred with and learned from. The first time Windu managed to best one of his instructors came with Saa, who was surprised but respected his skill, creating a fond memory for the blossoming Jedi. Windu would also develop a long lasting friendship with [Sora Bulq](/wiki/Sora_Bulq "Sora Bulq"), a fellow Jedi.[[8]](#cite_note-Glass_Abyss-8)

#### Mission to Mathas

:   "*A fire burns inside you, Padawan. That, in itself, is not inherently wrong. It is my job to help you temper it. This is why I chose you to accompany me on this mission. I do so enjoy a challenge.*"
:   ―Cyslin Myr, to Mace Windu[[6]](#cite_note-JoRMW4-6)

 [![Padawan Windu was trained in the ways of the Force by Jedi Master Cyslin Myr.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2e/MyrWinduHissrich-JOTRMaceWindu4.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190118020829) [![Padawan Windu was trained in the ways of the Force by Jedi Master Cyslin Myr.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2e/MyrWinduHissrich-JOTRMaceWindu4.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190118020829)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2e/MyrWinduHissrich-JOTRMaceWindu4.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190118020829) 

Padawan Windu was trained in the ways of the Force by Jedi Master Cyslin Myr.

 

Following his early trials as a youngling, Windu attained the status of [Padawan](/wiki/Padawan "Padawan") by becoming [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") [Cyslin Myr](/wiki/Cyslin_Myr "Cyslin Myr")'s apprentice. During Windu's apprenticeship[[6]](#cite_note-JoRMW4-6) in [60 BBY](/wiki/60_BBY "60 BBY"),[[3]](#cite_note-Timelines-3) a man named [Drooz](/wiki/Drooz "Drooz") had taken residence in a Jedi [outreach temple](/wiki/Outreach_temple "Outreach temple") on the planet [Mathas](/wiki/Mathas "Mathas"). With the local populace suffering from the effects of the [Niffin plague](/wiki/Niffin_plague "Niffin plague"), Drooz convinced the people that he was a Jedi [prophet](/wiki/Prophet "Prophet") who could heal the sick and the dying in return for their faith and servitude. Upon receiving reports of Drooz's activities, the Order dispatched Myr on a [mission](/wiki/Mission_to_Mathas "Mission to Mathas") to assess and apprehend him. At the same time, Myr sought to teach Windu how to channel his frustrations into an appropriate emotion and therefore brought him to Mathas.[[6]](#cite_note-JoRMW4-6)

As they made their way to the [temple](/wiki/Jedi_temple "Jedi temple"), Windu observed the people's situation and pondered on what the Jedi could do to alleviate their suffering. He also denounced Drooz as a heretic and swindler who perverted the Jedi doctrine in order to take advantage of the people's misery. At that point his Master cautioned him to suppress his hostile feelings, having noticed how the thought of Drooz using the Jedi's teachings to prey on others frustrated Windu. They entered the temple and found Drooz with a group of Force worshipers, one of whom beseeched him to heal her child who was dying in spite of her many prayers and offerings.[[6]](#cite_note-JoRMW4-6)

Drooz's followers came to his defense when the Jedi openly confronted him. Using the distraction they created, he tried to escape from the temple but was pursued by Windu. Although Drooz's [Gamorrean](/wiki/Gamorrean "Gamorrean") [bodyguards](/wiki/Bodyguard "Bodyguard") were defeated by the Padawan, Drooz managed to injure Windu's left [arm](/wiki/Limb "Limb") with his [blaster pistol](/wiki/Blaster_pistol "Blaster pistol"). He taunted Windu and mocked the Jedi's ways, sneering at their commitment to peace as he believed they should use their power to gain wealth through the faith of millions. Using the Force to immobilize Drooz, Windu disarmed him and vowed that he would never hurt anyone else. However, Myr intervened by ordering Windu to lower his lightsaber. While she understood her apprentice's frustrations, Myr believed that Drooz's punishment should be decided in a court of law.[[6]](#cite_note-JoRMW4-6)

### Knight of the Order

#### Various work

Windu eventually continued training under the guidance of Yoda[[11]](#cite_note-CVD-11) and eventually ascended into a Jedi Knight and partook in various assignments throughout the galaxy.[[18]](#cite_note-Rev23-18) At some point during his service to the Jedi Order, Windu, recognizing that an internal darkness existed within him, created the [Vaapad form of lightsaber combat](/wiki/Form_VII "Form VII")[[19]](#cite_note-Knights_Fate-19) with help from Sora Bulq[[8]](#cite_note-Glass_Abyss-8) to channel that darkness to better outcomes.[[19]](#cite_note-Knights_Fate-19) He also began holding lessons regarding letting go and trusting into the Force.[[17]](#cite_note-Queen's_Peril-17)

#### Investigating Mattis Coto

During a specific mission, Windu was assigned to [investigate](/wiki/Mission_to_Devshi "Mission to Devshi") [Mattis Coto](/wiki/Mattis_Coto "Mattis Coto"), the [warden](/wiki/Warden "Warden") of the [Devshi prison complex](/wiki/Devshi_prison_complex "Devshi prison complex"), due to suspicions of his involvement in the illicit trade of skeleton keys. This suspicion arose after the apprehension of convicts in [Kevan 8](/wiki/Kevan_8 "Kevan 8"), where one of the prisoners claimed to have received a skeleton key from Coto. Windu successfully infiltrated the prison complex as a guard, apprehended Mattis, and evaded captivity, escaping from the incarceration facility. Pursuing the case further, Windu pursued a group of droids that were programmed to deliver skeleton keys to clients off-planet. Employing his formidable abilities and lightsaber, Windu utilized a mind trick to gain the assistance of [Regump](/wiki/Regump "Regump"), an impromptu skiff pilot. Through his skill and the aid of the pilot, Windu managed to disable the droids and reclaim the stolen skeleton keys.[[18]](#cite_note-Rev23-18)[[20]](#cite_note-Windu1-20)

#### Race for Coaxium Ultra

Following his previous mission, Windu returned to the Jedi Temple to provide a report on his successful completion to Master Yoda. During this meeting, Master Yoda, along with Jedi Knight [Gara](/wiki/Gara "Gara"), assigned Windu his [next task](/wiki/Mission_to_Ro_Mira "Mission to Ro Mira"): the recovery of the [coaxium ultra](/wiki/Coaxium_ultra "Coaxium ultra") formula from a smuggler named [Azita Cruuz](/wiki/Azita_Cruuz "Azita Cruuz"). It was revealed that Azita had offered the formula to the Jedi Order and criminal organizations in exchange for Republic credits and a safe passage offworld from Ro Mira. Windu discovered that the formula, if obtained by the wrong individuals, could grant criminal elements a significant advantage, as coaxium ultra had the potential to boost sublight engines by 120% without consequences. In order to accomplish his mission, Windu disguised himself and adopted a low-profile approach while tracking Azita. Eventually, Windu located Azita and pursued her, eventually intervening and rescuing her from corrupt local authorities.[[20]](#cite_note-Windu1-20)

During their attempt to escape off-world, Windu becomes acquainted with Azita's backstory. She had encountered a client who was aware of Doctor Bishop's work, which involved refining the coaxium formula by relocating to Ro Mira, a planet known for its blue fire lava that enhances the results of coaxium. Azita assisted the scientist in developing the formula but also administered a drug obtained on Coruscant to induce temporary sleep and erase his memory of the past six months. While Windu views Azita's actions as morally questionable, she argues that circumstances often force people into actions against their will, drawing a parallel to Windu's own path as a Jedi and questioning if he had willingly chosen it. Their discussion is interrupted by the presence of bore worms, creatures that are resistant to lightsabers. Windu relies on the Force to neutralize them, a decision that Azita criticizes. Windu explains that he spared the bore worms because they were acting as animals without malicious intent, comparing the purpose of a lightsaber to that of a shield. He also responds to Azita's earlier question about his service to the Jedi Order, admitting that while he did not consciously volunteer, he has not dwelled on the alternative life he might have had, considering it futile and potentially dangerous. Windu believes that his current path is where he is meant to be. Azita, still uncertain about whom she will sell the formula to, becomes more open to the idea of selling it to someone from their shared homeworld of Haruun Kal, deducing their common background based on the inoculation scars they both bear from their time as toddlers on Haruun Kal. As the pair continues their escape, with Azita unsure if she can fully trust Windu, they find themselves pursued by members of the Shroud.[[15]](#cite_note-Windu2-15)

### Rising through the ranks

After translating an encrypted message sent out by [Depa Billaba](/wiki/Depa_Billaba "Depa Billaba"),[[21]](#cite_note-Odyssey-21) Windu rescued both Billaba and [Sar Labooda](/wiki/Sar_Labooda "Sar Labooda") from [pirates](/wiki/Pirate "Pirate"),[[12]](#cite_note-The_Secret_Jedi-12) using his lightsaber in combat during the incident.[[21]](#cite_note-Odyssey-21) He brought both sisters[[22]](#cite_note-Women_of_the_Galaxy-22) to the Jedi Temple on Coruscant and trained Billaba in the Jedi arts until she attained the rank of Jedi Knight.[[12]](#cite_note-The_Secret_Jedi-12) As a Jedi Master, he also held lessons around letting go and trusting in the Force as he did as a Jedi Knight.[[17]](#cite_note-Queen's_Peril-17) By [40 BBY](/wiki/40_BBY "40 BBY"),[[23]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice_date-23) Billaba was serving on the High Council alongside her former Master.[[24]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-24)

#### Councilor of the Order

:   "*I am told that you will be presented with Master Katri's Council seat.*"  
    "*I will.*"  
    "*Is this something you knew was happening before we left for Raxus?*"  
    "*I was as surprised as you are now. Dooku, you and I both were together when the mission was assigned. I stuck to the mission. You decided to interfere in a way that led to a senator's death. I will speak to the Council on your behalf.*"  
    "*How kind of you, Master Jedi.*"
:   ―Dooku and Mace Windu[[25]](#cite_note-TOTJ-Choices-25)

 [![The Jedi Windu and Dooku were attacked by a group of disgruntled security guards, who were responsible for the death of Jedi Master Katri.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7c/Choices.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20221026194431) [![The Jedi Windu and Dooku were attacked by a group of disgruntled security guards, who were responsible for the death of Jedi Master Katri.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7c/Choices.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20221026194431)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7c/Choices.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20221026194431) 

The Jedi Windu and Dooku were attacked by a group of disgruntled security guards, who were responsible for the death of Jedi Master Katri.

 

Sometime later, he became a Jedi Master and gained a seat on the [Jedi High Council](/wiki/Jedi_High_Council "Jedi High Council")—the governing body of the Jedi Order,[[9]](#cite_note-TPM-9) between [50 BBY](/wiki/50_BBY "50 BBY") and [42 BBY](/wiki/42_BBY "42 BBY"),[[26]](#cite_note-Choices_date-26) as a result of the mission on [Raxus Secundus](/wiki/Raxus_Secundus "Raxus Secundus"), where Jedi Master [Katri](/wiki/Katri "Katri") was killed. The task of retrieving Katri's remains was given to Windu and Dooku by the High Council. Unsatisfied with [Senator](/wiki/Senator "Senator") [Larik](/wiki/Larik "Larik")'s testimony regarding an ambush that killed Katri, Dooku sought to conduct his own investigation. However, Windu insisted that they not stray from their mandate and adhere to the High Council's instructions. He also reminded Dooku that as neither of them were members of the High Council, they did not possess the authority to interfere in political conflicts without the blessings of their Council or the [Galactic Senate](/wiki/Galactic_Senate "Galactic Senate"). Although Dooku regarded Windu as a friend, he considered his colleague's strict devotion to Jedi protocol "inspiring and maddening."[[25]](#cite_note-TOTJ-Choices-25)

Windu and Dooku met with Senator Larik in [Raxulon](/wiki/Raxulon "Raxulon"). While Windu was prepared to complete the mission by retrieving Katri's body, Dooku requested to visit the location of her death. The senator was reluctant to comply until one of his security guards, [Semage](/wiki/Semage "Semage"), agreed to escort the Jedi. Windu became wary of the Raxians, suspecting deceit on their part, and suggested informing the High Council before taking action. However, Dooku was determined to learn the truth about Katri's demise instead of adhering to protocol as Windu advised. Upon investigating the area where Katri died, the Jedi concluded that the evidence did not support the Raxians' account. Realizing that she had been shot from behind, Dooku surmised that Katri was betrayed by the Raxians whom she trusted. Windu tried to deescalate the situation when Dooku activated [his lightsaber](/wiki/Dooku%27s_lightsaber "Dooku's lightsaber") demanding the truth. In a panic, Senator Larik confessed that his own guards murdered Katri and attempted to reach the Jedi, but was fatally shot by one of his officers. A skirmish ensued between the Jedi and the Raxians; the Jedi Masters worked together to destroy the Raxians' [droid](/wiki/Raxus_Droid "Raxus Droid") support before neutralizing the guards. [Hanel](/wiki/Hanel "Hanel") was killed by a stray blast that Windu deflected when the officer attacked him, and Semage was taken into custody.[[25]](#cite_note-TOTJ-Choices-25)

 [![Returning from Raxus Secundus, Windu attended the funeral of Master Katri and was granted her seat on the Jedi High Council.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/16/KatriFuneral-Choices.png/revision/latest?cb=20221104052846) [![Returning from Raxus Secundus, Windu attended the funeral of Master Katri and was granted her seat on the Jedi High Council.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/16/KatriFuneral-Choices.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20221104052846)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/16/KatriFuneral-Choices.png/revision/latest?cb=20221104052846) 

Returning from Raxus Secundus, Windu attended the funeral of Master Katri and was granted her seat on the Jedi High Council.

 

Semage accused the Jedi of protecting the interests of a corrupt Senate. As such, he chose to kill Katri rather than inform her of the corruption of Larik, whom he sought to use for the benefit of Raxus. Windu contested the officer's opinion in stating that as a Jedi, Katri would have listened to Semage. Windu and Dooku later attended the [funeral of Katri](/wiki/Funeral_of_Katri "Funeral of Katri") at the [Jedi Temple](/wiki/Imperial_Palace "Imperial Palace") on [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant"). Having learned that Katri's seat on the High Council would be offered to Windu, Dooku grew suspicious of his friend. Windu insisted he was as surprised as Dooku was about his elevation to the High Council's ranks. Furthermore, Windu reminded Dooku that they had both received their orders from the High Council, and it was Dooku who pursued a course of action that resulted in the death of a Republic senator. Nevertheless, Windu assured Dooku that he would speak on his behalf to the High Council.[[25]](#cite_note-TOTJ-Choices-25)

Long regarded[[4]](#cite_note-Databank-4) as the Jedi Order's greatest champion,[[27]](#cite_note-Windu's_Lightsaber-27) Windu endeavored to maintain the Jedi's ancient traditions while the Republic declined due to [galactic](/wiki/Galaxy "Galaxy") unrest and political corruption.[[4]](#cite_note-Databank-4) As one of the most distinctive members of the Order,[[27]](#cite_note-Windu's_Lightsaber-27) Windu crafted a new lightsaber which—in addition to its specially designed handgrip and [electrum](/wiki/Electrum "Electrum") finish, indicating his status as a member of the High Council[[28]](#cite_note-USW-28)—also emitted a [plasma](/wiki/Plasma "Plasma") blade of amethyst, making it [one of the most distinctive Jedi weapons](/wiki/Mace_Windu%27s_lightsaber "Mace Windu's lightsaber").[[27]](#cite_note-Windu's_Lightsaber-27) At some point, he also became the elected leader of the Council, serving alongside Yoda as [Master of the Order](/wiki/Master_of_the_Order "Master of the Order").[[29]](#cite_note-Insider_199-29) He was also a [Jedi Vanguard](/wiki/Jedi_Vanguard "Jedi Vanguard").[[30]](#cite_note-GoH-30)

#### Ontotho uprising

 [![Due to her heroic acts on Ontotho, Mace Windu promotes Cere Junda and performs the Knighting Ceremony, making her a Jedi Knight.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b2/CereJundaGetsKnighted-JFODarkTemple5.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20220405102835) [![Due to her heroic acts on Ontotho, Mace Windu promotes Cere Junda and performs the Knighting Ceremony, making her a Jedi Knight.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b2/CereJundaGetsKnighted-JFODarkTemple5.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220405102835)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b2/CereJundaGetsKnighted-JFODarkTemple5.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20220405102835) 

Due to her heroic acts on Ontotho, Mace Windu promotes Cere Junda and performs the Knighting Ceremony, making her a Jedi Knight.

 

In [41 BBY](/wiki/41_BBY "41 BBY"),[[3]](#cite_note-Timelines-3) Windu was among the councilors to hear Padawan [Junda's](/wiki/Cere_Junda "Cere Junda") account of her actions while she and Master [Cordova](/wiki/Eno_Cordova "Eno Cordova") attempted to settle a dispute on [Nameel](/wiki/Nameel "Nameel") between [Dupei monks](/wiki/Dupei_monks "Dupei monks") and [Trandoshans](/wiki/Trandoshan "Trandoshan"), where the monks admitted to provoking them by stealing their credits but the Trandoshans provoked her into self-defense. Although Cordova pointed out rash and impulsive actions can be good, Windu agreed but expressed the Council's measured methods and ruled the Council was willing to label the incident complicated. He then gave them their next assignment, tasking Cordova and Junda with working alongside the [Daa Corporation](/wiki/Daa_Corporation "Daa Corporation") in uncovering an ancient temple given the former's specialty in ancient cultures.[[31]](#cite_note-Dark_Temple_1-31)

Windu would later arrive when the Daa Corporation and the [Flyari](/wiki/Fylari "Fylari")'s dispute escalated into a civil conflict and prompted a intervention by the Republic alongside Jedi Masters [Luminara](/wiki/Luminara_Unduli "Luminara Unduli"), [Maslo-Scaff](/wiki/Maslo-Skaff "Maslo-Skaff"), and [Odu](/wiki/Odu "Odu"). Reunited with Junda, the Jedi helped quelled the situation, ending the conflict by exposing Daa Coporation's corruption to be dealt with in Republic courts and the Flyari agreeing to help create a new joint-government. Due to Junda's heroic actions, she was promoted to Jedi Knight, the [Knighting Ceremony](/wiki/Knighting_Ceremony "Knighting Ceremony") performed by Windu himself.[[32]](#cite_note-Dark_Temple_5-32)

### Mission to Oosalon

:   "*And what of Quia, Master Yoda? She is a young enough orphan that perhaps she could find a new home.*"  
    "*No. Face imprisonment for her role in terrorist attacks, she will. Interfere in local laws, we cannot.*"  
    "*Then we didn't save* everyone*… did we?*"
:   ―Mace Windu and Yoda[[14]](#cite_note-Age_of_Republic-14)

 [![Windu's capture was part of the Jedi's strategy to locate the camp of the warlord Guattako.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1e/MaceWinduGetsKnockedOut-TheWeapon.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190122041733) [![Windu's capture was part of the Jedi's strategy to locate the camp of the warlord Guattako.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1e/MaceWinduGetsKnockedOut-TheWeapon.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190122041733)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1e/MaceWinduGetsKnockedOut-TheWeapon.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190122041733) 

Windu's capture was part of the Jedi's strategy to locate the camp of the warlord Guattako.

 

In [34 BBY](/wiki/34_BBY "34 BBY"),[[3]](#cite_note-Timelines-3) The Jedi Order deployed Mace Windu along with several other Jedi on a mission to the [Outer Rim](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Territories "Outer Rim Territories") planet of [Oosalon](/wiki/Oosalon "Oosalon") due to the [terrorist](/wiki/Terrorist "Terrorist") attacks committed by [Guattako's army](/wiki/Guattako%27s_army "Guattako's army"). He allowed himself to be captured and taken to [Guattako](/wiki/Guattako "Guattako") in order to discover the location of the [warlord](/wiki/Warlord "Warlord")'s base of operations, which was hidden in 80,000 [kilometers](/wiki/Kilometer "Kilometer") of [cavernous](/wiki/Cave "Cave") tunnels. Windu, having learned that Guattako's operation relied on using orphans and kidnapped children as soldiers, tried to convince the child [Quia](/wiki/Quia "Quia") to renounce the insurgents and their war against the government of Oosalon.[[14]](#cite_note-Age_of_Republic-14)

Windu denounced [Guattako](/wiki/Guattako "Guattako") as a terrorist and a kidnapper who relied on the [Hutt Clan](/wiki/Hutt_Clan "Hutt Clan") to financially support his cause. With Windu's lightsaber broken down to its components, Guattako was confident in his ability to detain the Jedi Master whom he intended to execute, believing that Windu's death would inspire others to join his fledgling group. By the time he realized that Windu had planned on getting captured, the Jedi had reassembled his lightsaber through the Force. He also revealed that he had used the Force to help his fellow Jedi find the insurgents' camp.[[14]](#cite_note-Age_of_Republic-14)

 [![Windu and his fellow Jedi succeeded in disrupting the terrorist operations of the warlord Guattako.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/02/JediOnOosalon-TheWeapon.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190418005506) [![Windu and his fellow Jedi succeeded in disrupting the terrorist operations of the warlord Guattako.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/02/JediOnOosalon-TheWeapon.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190418005506)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/02/JediOnOosalon-TheWeapon.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190418005506) 

Windu and his fellow Jedi succeeded in disrupting the terrorist operations of the warlord Guattako.

 

Windu successfully defended himself against Quia and the other insurgents before engaging Guattako in single combat. During the battle, Guattako was fatally shot by one of the abducted children who wanted to return to his home. By then, the other Jedi arrived at Windu's location. With the Jedi's assistance, the remaining insurgents were taken into custody by the security forces of Oosalon. Although the Jedi had succeeded in rescuing twenty-six abducted school children, Windu had also hoped to save Quia and the child soldiers who were already indoctrinated into Guattako's cause. However, Yoda stated that the Jedi could not interfere in the planet's local affairs, and that Quia would be sent to [prison](/wiki/Prison "Prison") for her part in Guattako's terrorist campaign. Windu accepted the outcome, but lamented on not being able to help Quia.[[14]](#cite_note-Age_of_Republic-14)

### Invasion of Naboo

:   "*There's no doubt the mysterious warrior was a Sith."  
    "Always two, there are. No more, no less. A master and an apprentice."  
    "But which was destroyed, the master or the apprentice?*"
:   ―Mace Windu and Yoda, on the return of the Sith — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/56/AlwaysTwoThereAre-TPM.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250407192606)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:AlwaysTwoThereAre-TPM.flac "File:AlwaysTwoThereAre-TPM.flac"))[[9]](#cite_note-TPM-9)

 [![Windu served on the Jedi High Council during the decline of the Galactic Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/45/Mace_Windu_Jedi_Council_TPM.png/revision/latest?cb=20130118052819) [![Windu served on the Jedi High Council during the decline of the Galactic Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/45/Mace_Windu_Jedi_Council_TPM.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/284?cb=20130118052819)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/45/Mace_Windu_Jedi_Council_TPM.png/revision/latest?cb=20130118052819) 

Windu served on the Jedi High Council during the decline of the Galactic Republic.

 

Approximately ten years before the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars"),[[9]](#cite_note-TPM-9) Windu, [hours](/wiki/Standard_hour "Standard hour") after attending a Council meeting, found Yoda alone in a small garden in the Jedi Temple. Denying Yoda's joke about whether he had an embarrassing question he couldn't ask in front of the Council, he questioned whether the Grand Master had sensed something he had not told them of. Yoda explained he was instead sensing a lack of something, much to the confusion of Windu, leading to a debate about the concepts of "nothing" and "something." Deciding the Force would educate him in due time, Windu decided to trust Yoda's judgement, leaving the room after not speaking for several minutes.[[17]](#cite_note-Queen's_Peril-17)

Later, the [Trade Federation](/wiki/Trade_Federation "Trade Federation") initiated a [blockade](/wiki/Blockade "Blockade") of the planet [Naboo](/wiki/Naboo "Naboo"). At the request of [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor") [Finis Valorum](/wiki/Finis_Valorum "Finis Valorum"), the Jedi Council ordered [Qui-Gon Jinn](/wiki/Qui-Gon_Jinn "Qui-Gon Jinn") and his apprentice, [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi"), to settle the dispute as emissaries of the chancellor. Upon returning from their failed mission, the Council was made aware of a far greater threat, the ancient enemy of the Jedi—the [Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith")—had returned.[[9]](#cite_note-TPM-9)

However, neither Mace Windu or [Ki-Adi-Mundi](/wiki/Ki-Adi-Mundi "Ki-Adi-Mundi") were particularly convinced that the Jedi Order's ancient nemesis could have returned, much less avoid the awareness of the Jedi Council. Nevertheless, Windu assured them that the full resources of the Order would be utilized to verify the truth of Jinn's claims—and more specifically, the identity of the [dark warrior](/wiki/Maul "Maul") who [attacked](/wiki/Duel_on_Tatooine "Duel on Tatooine") him on [Tatooine](/wiki/Tatooine "Tatooine"). It was then that Jinn revealed another significant discovery that he made during the course of his mission. Prior to his departure from Tatooine and subsequent return to Coruscant, Jinn encountered [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker"). Unknown to the Jedi, the [slave](/wiki/Slavery "Slavery") [Shmi Skywalker](/wiki/Shmi_Skywalker_Lars "Shmi Skywalker Lars") had given birth to a son who was exceptionally powerful with the Force; because of Anakin's inherent potential and the circumstances surrounding his birth, Jinn believed Anakin could have been conceived by the [midi-chlorians](/wiki/Midi-chlorian "Midi-chlorian").[[9]](#cite_note-TPM-9)

Windu knew that Jinn referred to the Jedi prophecy of the [Chosen One](/wiki/Chosen_One "Chosen One")—The One who would restore balance to the Force[[9]](#cite_note-TPM-9) by destroying the Sith.[[33]](#cite_note-ROTS-33) Although Skywalker possessed the highest concentration of midi-chlorians in his [cells](/wiki/DNA "DNA"), Windu was skeptical of Jinn's claims, but nonetheless agreed to meet the boy in the Council's [chamber](/wiki/Jedi_Council_Chamber "Jedi Council Chamber") where they would evaluate his aptitude with the Force. The Council was impressed by Skywalker's ability to use the Force without any formal training, but they also sensed his emotional attachment to his [mother](/wiki/Parent "Parent") and a great amount of fear within him. As such, they declined Jinn's request to have him trained in the Jedi arts.[[9]](#cite_note-TPM-9) Windu personally felt that Skywalker was too old to commit his life to the [Jedi Code](/wiki/Jedi_Code "Jedi Code"), as well as the Force, without the distraction of his emotional attachments.[[4]](#cite_note-Databank-4) Nevertheless, despite his doubts of Jinn's claim, he tasked him and his apprentice to investigate the identity of the dark warrior, believing the election of a new Supreme Chancellor would draw him out and would provide a crucial clue to the "mystery of the Sith."[[9]](#cite_note-TPM-9)

The Council soon reversed its decision after Jinn's [death](/wiki/Death "Death") during the [Battle of Naboo](/wiki/Battle_of_Naboo "Battle of Naboo"), entrusting Skywalker's training to the newly-anointed Jedi Knight Obi-Wan Kenobi.[[9]](#cite_note-TPM-9) Windu continued to doubt Skywalker's ability to commit himself to the Jedi way, however, and his ill-concealed distrust would put a strain on their relationship throughout the years as Skywalker ascended the ranks of the Jedi Order.[[4]](#cite_note-Databank-4) During the [funeral of Qui-Gon Jinn](/wiki/Funeral_of_Qui-Gon_Jinn "Funeral of Qui-Gon Jinn"), which the Naboo waited to begin until the arrival of the Jedi Council,[[17]](#cite_note-Queen's_Peril-17) Yoda and Windu realized that Jinn had been correct; the Sith had indeed survived and endured over the last millennium. Yoda quoted the [Rule of Two](/wiki/Rule_of_Two "Rule of Two"), an ancient Sith philosophy that limited their ranks to two [Sith Lords](/wiki/Sith_Lord "Sith Lord")—a [master](/wiki/Sith_Master "Sith Master") and an [apprentice](/wiki/Sith_apprentice "Sith apprentice")—causing Windu to ponder over which of the two was defeated by Kenobi.[[9]](#cite_note-TPM-9) When Jinn's body had turned to ash,[[17]](#cite_note-Queen's_Peril-17) Windu[[9]](#cite_note-TPM-9) and the other Council members left the funeral.[[17]](#cite_note-Queen's_Peril-17) Afterward, he attended the victory celebration on Naboo along with Yoda, several members of the Jedi Council, and the newly-elected Supreme Chancellor [Sheev Palpatine](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious").[[9]](#cite_note-TPM-9)

### Training Skywalker

#### Overseeing Skywalker's advancement

:   "*Remember, Obi-Wan. If the prophecy is true, your apprentice is the only one who can bring the Force back into balance.*"
:   ―Mace Windu, to Obi-Wan Kenobi[[7]](#cite_note-AOTC-7)

 [![Anakin Skywalker's path to Jedi Knighthood was closely monitored by Windu, Obi-Wan Kenobi, and Supreme Chancellor Sheev Palpatine.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2d/WinduPalpatineKenobi-ObiWanAnakin1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210623060421) [![Anakin Skywalker's path to Jedi Knighthood was closely monitored by Windu, Obi-Wan Kenobi, and Supreme Chancellor Sheev Palpatine.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2d/WinduPalpatineKenobi-ObiWanAnakin1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/297?cb=20210623060421)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2d/WinduPalpatineKenobi-ObiWanAnakin1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210623060421) 

Anakin Skywalker's path to Jedi Knighthood was closely monitored by Windu, Obi-Wan Kenobi, and Supreme Chancellor Sheev Palpatine.

 

The training of Anakin Skywalker drew the attention of his peers, Padawans and Jedi Masters alike, as well as Chancellor Palpatine, during his first three years as Kenobi's apprentice. He especially took an interest in [lightsaber combat](/wiki/Lightsaber_combat "Lightsaber combat"), as noted by Palpatine, although Windu was more focused on the [training droid](/wiki/Jedi_training_droid "Jedi training droid")—mimicking the appearance and fighting style of Darth Maul—that Skywalker sparred with. Neither Windu or Kenobi had expected to see Skywalker duel with the visage of Maul, but the act served to impress Palpatine.[[34]](#cite_note-O&A_1-34)

However, Kenobi was forced to intervene after Skywalker used the Force to take the lightsabers of two nearby apprentices, having overheard them mocking him for being a "slave to his emotions." Windu observed the incident as an example of how Skywalker was a complicated case for the Jedi, given the fact that he joined the Order far later than any of his contemporaries. After mentioning that Skywalker's training was an extremely difficult task for Kenobi, Windu politely declined the chancellor's offer to help guide the young Jedi. However, Palpatine claimed that as the Jedi were under the jurisdiction of the Senate, by extension they also reported to the Senate's chancellor. After considering Palpatine's line of reasoning, Windu agreed to send Skywalker to speak with the chancellor.[[34]](#cite_note-O&A_1-34)

#### Testing Kenobi and Skywalker

In [26 BBY](/wiki/26_BBY "26 BBY"),[[3]](#cite_note-Timelines-3) Windu was involved in a [test](/wiki/Rescue_of_Yoda "Rescue of Yoda") of the master and apprenticeship of Kenobi and Skywalker, partnering with Yoda and Jedi Master [Bant Eerin](/wiki/Bant_Eerin "Bant Eerin") to feign the kidnapping of the Grandmaster.[[35]](#cite_note-Choose_Your_Destiny-35) In the days leading up to the start of the Clone Wars, the High Council was confident that Skywalker was ready to be given a mission of his own for the first time. By then, Windu regarded him as an exceptionally skilled Jedi, but Kenobi was concerned that his Padawan's abilities led him to become arrogant and therefore had much to learn. Yoda concurred with Kenobi, but also felt that Skywalker was not an isolated case. In his assessment, other Jedi had grown overconfident in their skills as well. At this, Windu told Kenobi to keep the prophecy in mind, for if Skywalker was indeed the Chosen One then only he could bring the Force back into a state of balance.[[7]](#cite_note-AOTC-7)

### Clone Wars

#### Prelude to war

:   "*You must realize there aren't enough Jedi to protect the Republic. We are keepers of the peace, not soldiers.*"
:   ―Mace Windu, to Sheev Palpatine[[7]](#cite_note-AOTC-7)

 [![Windu warned Palpatine that the Jedi Order lacked the manpower to protect the Republic in the event of war.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/FiveFamousJediContinueToFailToDetectTheSith-AotC.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20060202113336) [![Windu warned Palpatine that the Jedi Order lacked the manpower to protect the Republic in the event of war.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/FiveFamousJediContinueToFailToDetectTheSith-AotC.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/270?cb=20060202113336)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/FiveFamousJediContinueToFailToDetectTheSith-AotC.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20060202113336) 

Windu warned Palpatine that the Jedi Order lacked the manpower to protect the Republic in the event of war.

 

In the [decade](/wiki/Standard_decade "Standard decade") that followed the Battle of Naboo, the Galactic Republic faced an [existential crisis](/wiki/Separatist_Crisis "Separatist Crisis") as thousands of [star systems](/wiki/Star_system "Star system") and powerful corporations threatened to secede from the ancient [democratic](/wiki/Democracy "Democracy") union. Chancellor Palpatine assured the Jedi Council that his office was seeking a peaceful resolution with the Separatists, and that he would not permit secession to divide the millennium-old Republic. Despite the chancellor's assurances, Mace Windu advised him to consider just how vulnerable the Republic truly was—the Jedi Order lacked the sufficient manpower to defend the entire Republic in the event of war. Moreover, the Order was a force of peacekeepers rather than [soldiers](/wiki/Soldier "Soldier").[[7]](#cite_note-AOTC-7)

As the Galactic Senate continued to debate over whether to vote for or against the proposed [Military Creation Act](/wiki/Military_Creation_Act "Military Creation Act"), Senator [Padmé Amidala](/wiki/Padm%C3%A9_Amidala "Padmé Amidala") narrowly avoided an [assassination](/wiki/Assassin "Assassin") attempt on her life. During a meeting with the chancellor, she revealed to Windu and Yoda her suspicion that [Count](/wiki/Count "Count") [Dooku](/wiki/Dooku "Dooku") was involved in the attack. Although Dooku had renounced his Jedi status before becoming the leader of the Separatist movement, Windu refused to believe that even a former Jedi could be involved in a plot to assassinate the Naboo senator—or anyone for that matter. Nevertheless, Windu heeded Yoda and Palpatine's warning that Amidala's life was in grave danger, regardless of whether Dooku was personally involved or not. As such, he dispatched Obi-Wan Kenobi and Anakin Skywalker to serve as temporary bodyguards for the senator. After the death of Amidala's would-be assassin, [Zam Wesell](/wiki/Zam_Wesell "Zam Wesell"), Windu and the Council instructed Kenobi to track Wesell's accomplice who evaded capture. They also ordered Skywalker to accompany Amidala to her [home planet](/wiki/Homeworld "Homeworld") of Naboo in case of another assassination attempt against her.[[7]](#cite_note-AOTC-7)

While the Separatist Crisis worsened, Windu concurred with Yoda's belief that the [dark side of the Force](/wiki/Dark_side_of_the_Force "Dark side of the Force") was responsible for the turmoil that undermined galactic peace and stability.[[4]](#cite_note-Databank-4) They were especially disturbed to learn that Kenobi's investigation led him to the planet [Kamino](/wiki/Kamino "Kamino") where their agent discovered the existence of a secret [army](/wiki/Army "Army")—hundreds of thousands of [clone troopers](/wiki/Clone_trooper "Clone trooper"), in addition to a million more units in development. [Prime Minister](/wiki/Prime_Minister "Prime Minister") [Lama Su](/wiki/Lama_Su "Lama Su"), the leader of the [Kaminoan](/wiki/Kaminoan "Kaminoan") [cloners](/wiki/Scientist "Scientist"), revealed that the army was made to serve the Galactic Republic. He also asserted that the client who commissioned the project was the late Jedi Master [Sifo-Dyas](/wiki/Sifo-Dyas "Sifo-Dyas"), whom he presumed was alive and a leading member of the Jedi Council until Kenobi corrected his assumption.[[7]](#cite_note-AOTC-7)

 [![Kenobi's discovery of the clone army concerned Windu and Grand Master Yoda, both of whom were aware that the dark side clouded their collective vision.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cb/Mace_Yoda_holo.png/revision/latest?cb=20140722223200) [![Kenobi's discovery of the clone army concerned Windu and Grand Master Yoda, both of whom were aware that the dark side clouded their collective vision.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cb/Mace_Yoda_holo.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/268?cb=20140722223200)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cb/Mace_Yoda_holo.png/revision/latest?cb=20140722223200) 

Kenobi's discovery of the clone army concerned Windu and Grand Master Yoda, both of whom were aware that the dark side clouded their collective vision.

 

Kenobi followed the [source](/wiki/Clone_template "Clone template") of the clone army, the [bounty hunter](/wiki/Bounty_hunter "Bounty hunter") [Jango Fett](/wiki/Jango_Fett "Jango Fett"), to the planet [Geonosis](/wiki/Geonosis "Geonosis") where he reported another discovery to Windu and Yoda, both of whom witnessed his transmission in the [Chancellor's office](/wiki/Emperor%27s_office "Emperor's office"). Dooku and the [Separatist Council](/wiki/Executive_Separatist_Council "Executive Separatist Council") had no intention of negotiating a peaceful solution with the Republic; they merely stalled for [time](/wiki/Time "Time") in order to construct a [massive army](/wiki/Separatist_Droid_Army "Separatist Droid Army") of [battle droids](/wiki/Battle_droid "Battle droid") for one purpose—to wage war on the Republic. After the Senate voted to empower Chancellor Palpatine with emergency wartime powers, which he quickly used to authorize the formation of the [Grand Army of the Republic](/wiki/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic "Grand Army of the Republic"), Windu led a [Jedi assault team](/wiki/Jedi_assault_team "Jedi assault team") to Geonosis in order to rescue Kenobi while Yoda moved to take command of the clone [troopers](/wiki/Trooper "Trooper") on Kamino.[[7]](#cite_note-AOTC-7)

#### Battle of Geonosis

:   "*This party's over.*"
:   ―Mace Windu, confronting Count Dooku on Geonosis[[7]](#cite_note-AOTC-7)

 [![Jango Fett confronted the champion of the Jedi Order, a decision that led to the bounty hunter's decapitation by Windu's blade.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/54/Jangodied.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111022201552) [![Jango Fett confronted the champion of the Jedi Order, a decision that led to the bounty hunter's decapitation by Windu's blade.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/54/Jangodied.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/227?cb=20111022201552)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/54/Jangodied.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111022201552) 

Jango Fett confronted the champion of the Jedi Order, a decision that led to the bounty hunter's decapitation by Windu's blade.

 

Windu and the Jedi prevented the execution of Kenobi, as well as Skywalker and Amidala, both of whom traveled to Geonosis with the intention to help Kenobi, but were quickly confronted by an overwhelming force of battle [droids](/wiki/Droid "Droid").[[7]](#cite_note-AOTC-7) The Jedi fought bravely,[[4]](#cite_note-Databank-4) destroying many battle droids in the process, but also sustained a large number of casualties. During the fight, Windu swiftly killed Jango Fett with relative ease, decapitating the [bounty](/wiki/Bounty "Bounty") hunter, as [Boba Fett](/wiki/Boba_Fett "Boba Fett")—a clone whom Jango regarded as a son—watched in horror. Overwhelmed by the droids' superior numbers, the Jedi were cornered into the center of the [Geonosian](/wiki/Geonosian "Geonosian") [Petranaki Arena](/wiki/Petranaki_Arena "Petranaki Arena"). Dooku demanded that the Jedi surrender themselves into Separatist custody, but Windu refused to allow himself and his allies to be taken as prisoners of war. Moments later, the arrival of Yoda and the clone army ultimately turned the tide and enabled the Jedi survivors to escape the arena.[[7]](#cite_note-AOTC-7)

 [![Windu's rescue party was saved from slaughter by the arrival of Yoda and the Grand Army of the Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/10/Yoda_mace_windu_ki-adi-mundi_battle_of_geonosis.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111116045153) [![Windu's rescue party was saved from slaughter by the arrival of Yoda and the Grand Army of the Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/10/Yoda_mace_windu_ki-adi-mundi_battle_of_geonosis.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/249?cb=20111116045153)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/10/Yoda_mace_windu_ki-adi-mundi_battle_of_geonosis.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111116045153) 

Windu's rescue party was saved from slaughter by the arrival of Yoda and the Grand Army of the Republic.

 

In the aftermath of the arena skirmish, the [First Battle of Geonosis](/wiki/First_Battle_of_Geonosis "First Battle of Geonosis") officially commenced as thousands of clone troopers engaged the battle droids on the field of war. The remaining members of Windu's assault team took to the field as well, assuming command of the clones who were trained to serve the Jedi with absolute loyalty. Reporting directly to Windu, [Clone Commander](/wiki/Clone_Commander "Clone Commander") [Ponds](/wiki/Ponds "Ponds") and five special [commando](/wiki/Commando "Commando") units accompanied the legendary Jedi champion to the forefront of the battle.[[7]](#cite_note-AOTC-7) Windu kept Ponds by his side during the rest of the battle.[[36]](#cite_note-On_the_Front_Lines-36) Under the Jedi's leadership, the clone army forced the Separatists into full retreat, abandoning Geonosis to Republic occupation. Windu returned to the [capital](/wiki/Capital "Capital"), content that the first battle resulted in a Republic victory, but was also morose over the failure to capture Dooku.[[7]](#cite_note-AOTC-7) By then Windu came to accept that he had been wrong in his preconception of Dooku's character; his old friend had turned to the dark side, becoming an enemy of both the Order and the Republic.[[4]](#cite_note-Databank-4)

 [![After taking command of the clone troopers, Windu and his fellow Jedi secured the Republic's first victory in the Clone Wars.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3e/Jedi_Generals_Geonosis.png/revision/latest?cb=20180623160838) [![After taking command of the clone troopers, Windu and his fellow Jedi secured the Republic's first victory in the Clone Wars.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3e/Jedi_Generals_Geonosis.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20180623160838)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3e/Jedi_Generals_Geonosis.png/revision/latest?cb=20180623160838) 

After taking command of the clone troopers, Windu and his fellow Jedi secured the Republic's first victory in the Clone Wars.

 

The formation of the [Confederacy of Independent Systems](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems "Confederacy of Independent Systems") shattered a thousand years of peace that once defined the Jedi Order's role in the galaxy. In order to preserve and defend the Galactic Republic, Windu and his fellow Jedi accepted formal command of the clone army as [generals](/wiki/Jedi_General "Jedi General") and [commanders](/wiki/Commander "Commander"). He also learned from Kenobi about Dooku's assertion that a mysterious Sith [Lord](/wiki/Lord "Lord") by the name of [Darth](/wiki/Darth "Darth") Sidious had hundreds of senators under his control, but Yoda believed that the Council had no incentive to trust the word of a fallen Jedi. Windu nonetheless recommended that the Council maintain a watchful eye on the Senate,[[7]](#cite_note-AOTC-7) having never trusted the highly corrupt government in the first place.[[4]](#cite_note-Databank-4) As the clone troopers and their Jedi leaders prepared for war, Yoda expressed his sadness to Windu and Kenobi, declaring that the shroud of darkness had descended upon the galaxy—now engulfed by the Clone Wars, the first galactic-scale conflict since the formation of the Republic.[[7]](#cite_note-AOTC-7)

#### Mission to Hissrich

##### Deployed with his squad

:   "*You will lead a small unit to monitor the Separatists' and determine what their* purpose *is. Due to the clandestine nature of this mission and our thinly stretched resources, we cannot offer you a clone squadron for support.*"  
    "*The Jedi have trained our whole lives for missions like this. We will make do.*"
:   ―Plo Koon and Mace Windu[[10]](#cite_note-JoRMW1-10)

During the war, Windu mainly remained stationed on Coruscant.[[37]](#cite_note-TBotCW-37) However, he sometimes left the planet to perform special missions.[[10]](#cite_note-JoRMW1-10)

 [![Concerned by the Separatist activity on Hissrich, Windu investigated the planet with the help of a Jedi covert team.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/93/HissrichHologram-JOTRMaceWindu1.png/revision/latest?cb=20190117025136) [![Concerned by the Separatist activity on Hissrich, Windu investigated the planet with the help of a Jedi covert team.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/93/HissrichHologram-JOTRMaceWindu1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/211?cb=20190117025136)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/93/HissrichHologram-JOTRMaceWindu1.png/revision/latest?cb=20190117025136) 

Concerned by the Separatist activity on Hissrich, Windu investigated the planet with the help of a Jedi covert team.

 

Even in the early days of the Clone Wars, the High Council saw its situation as dire. With the Separatist army establishing multiple footholds throughout the Outer Rim, Windu was concerned that it would only be a matter of time before they moved inward, annexing more star systems before ultimately reaching the galactic capital of Coruscant. Seeking to ascertain the purpose of the Separatist presence on the planet [Hissrich](/wiki/Hissrich "Hissrich"), the Council assigned the task to Windu. However, because of the mission's covert purpose and the Republic's thinly spread resources, they were unable to provide him with a [squadron](/wiki/Squadron "Squadron") of clone troopers. Windu therefore assembled a [covert team](/wiki/Mace_Windu%27s_squad "Mace Windu's squad") of Jedi, consisting of himself along with [Kit Fisto](/wiki/Kit_Fisto "Kit Fisto"), for his skill with a lightsaber, [Prosset Dibs](/wiki/Tenth_Brother "Tenth Brother"), for his valuable insight and natural strong intuition with the Force, and [Rissa Mano](/wiki/Rissa_Mano "Rissa Mano"), for her [engineering](/wiki/Engineer "Engineer") skills and aptitude for battle.[[10]](#cite_note-JoRMW1-10)

After the council meeting, Yoda sensed Windu's troubles and asked if he could help. Windu explained how he felt doubt after the death of so many Jedi on Geonosis. Yoda then reassured him that the Force will always lead them down the correct path. The Grand Master told Windu that he must not give into these thoughts. Before departing, Windu promised that he would not fail him.[[10]](#cite_note-JoRMW1-10)

In transit, Mano told Windu that her ship was heavily modified for stealth and speed, to which Windu was thankful. Fisto remarked that he would be looking forward to working on this mission, but Dibs cynically replied that war was no place for a Jedi. To this, Mace said that they were Knights and this was exactly what they were supposed to be doing. After this, Windu notified the team of the undocumented nature of the planet and told them to be wary of fauna as well as battle droids. Mace also told them of the planets near constant darkness and how it would help them in their covert cause. When the alarm for exiting hyperspace sounded, Windu ordered them to change into their mission attire to help regulate body temperature.[[10]](#cite_note-JoRMW1-10)

Windu ordered them to use the plants as cover as they headed towards the nearest droid outpost. Dibs apologized for his previous outburst on the ship and explained it for his foresight of the teachings of their order being tested. Windu replied by saying sometimes combat is necessary and that war can breed confusion.[[10]](#cite_note-JoRMW1-10)

They soon encountered a small patrol group of a few B1 Battle droids and a Octupara droid. They quickly destroyed the patrol, but were soon surrounded by the indigenous people on all sides. Unknown to the strike team, a droid officer spotted the skirmish and reported it to [AD-W4](/wiki/AD-W4 "AD-W4"), a [mercenary](/wiki/Mercenary "Mercenary") droid hired by General Grievous to oversee the Separatist occupation of Hissrich.[[10]](#cite_note-JoRMW1-10)

After encountering members of Hissrich's [indigenous population](/wiki/Unidentified_Hissrich_species "Unidentified Hissrich species"), Windu and Fisto followed them into a system of [caverns](/wiki/Cave "Cave") and although they could not speak the [aliens](/wiki/Alien "Alien")' [language](/wiki/Language "Language"), Windu sensed that they were not hostile to the Jedi. The aliens led Windu and his team to their subterranean dwellings, at which point the Separatists attacked the Jedi after tracking their position to the alien settlement.[[38]](#cite_note-JoRMW2-38)

Windu ordered the other Jedi to protect the civilians while he fended off a group of [droidekas](/wiki/Droideka "Droideka") and [Single Trooper Aerial Platforms](/wiki/Single_Trooper_Aerial_Platform "Single Trooper Aerial Platform"). After dispatching the droids, he was confronted by AD-W4, who engaged the Jedi Master in single combat. As they fought, both combatants criticized their opponent's motivations; Windu regarded the droid's greed as a sign of depravity, whereas AD-W4 viewed the Jedi's beliefs—in particular, their commitment to peace—as asinine. During the fighting, the Jedi realized that the droids were mining the planet for its energy resources, the amount of which could turn the war in the Separatists' favor. Ultimately, a cave in separated the team in half, with Windu and Mano on the surface, while Fisto and Dibs were trapped below.[[38]](#cite_note-JoRMW2-38)

Together, Windu and Mano defeated the droids on the surface and succeeded in destroying one of the Separatist [harvesters](/wiki/Harvester_(Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems) "Harvester (Confederacy of Independent Systems)"). Afterward, they returned to their ship to regroup with Fisto and Dibs. At that point, Windu had determined that it would not be possible for his team to put an end to the Separatist operation one skirmish at a time, and therefore desired to locate the enemy's command center in order to bring the conflict on Hissrich to a swift and decisive conclusion.[[39]](#cite_note-JoRMW3-39)

##### Rebellion in the ranks

:   "*I have* failed *you, Prosset. I was to be your shepherd, and you have strayed too far from the path. All of these* bold accusations*, all of these grand* inquisitions*. If you think you know better than I what is good for the Jedi, what is good for the galaxy—*Then come! *Test your resolve against mine. Let us find out who is right.*"
:   ―Mace Windu, to Prosset Dibs[[39]](#cite_note-JoRMW3-39)

 [![Windu defeated Prosset Dibs, who was tried and found guilty of treason by the High Council.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/77/MaceWinduWins-JOTRMaceWindu4.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190118020848) [![Windu defeated Prosset Dibs, who was tried and found guilty of treason by the High Council.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/77/MaceWinduWins-JOTRMaceWindu4.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/295?cb=20190118020848)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/77/MaceWinduWins-JOTRMaceWindu4.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190118020848) 

Windu defeated Prosset Dibs, who was tried and found guilty of treason by the High Council.

 

The Jedi's mission on Hissrich was interrupted by a fallout that occurred between two of its members. Dibs confronted Windu soon after returning to the *Westwind* with Fisto; his doubts about their military role and the loss of multiple natives led him to lose faith in the Order and the High Council. Shouting at his fellow Jedi Master, Dibs made several accusations against both Windu and the Council, ranging from callousness towards collateral damage to distorting the Jedi doctrine. He then physically assaulted Windu, causing the High Council member to chastise Dibs for attacking his general.[[39]](#cite_note-JoRMW3-39)

Although Windu sympathized with Dibs' frustrations, he refused to entertain his claims, dismissing all of them as "bold accusations" and "grand inquisitions." Dibs took this as mockery and ignited his lightsaber, intending to take Windu's life. Realizing that Dibs would not back down, Windu declared that he had failed in his responsibility to keep Dibs on the Jedi path. He then accepted Dibs' challenge by igniting his own lightsaber.[[39]](#cite_note-JoRMW3-39) Yet even as they fought, Windu beseeched Dibs to cease his attack by reminding him that they were essentially brothers in the sense that they were both chosen to walk the path of the Jedi. Despite Dibs' resolve to kill Windu, he was ultimately disarmed and bested by the Jedi champion.[[6]](#cite_note-JoRMW4-6)

The ordeal served to remind Windu of his mission on Mathas years prior to the Clone Wars, in which he was tempted to take the life of the false prophet Drooz. Recalling his past experience with deciding another person's fate, Windu decided to arrest Dibs and to leave his punishment to the will of the High Council. After securing Dibs on the *Westwind*, the remaining Jedi proceeded to bring their mission to an end by attacking the AD-W4's headquarters. Although his own faith was tested during the duel, Dibs' accusations ultimately strengthened Windu's resolve and his belief that the Jedi Order existed to protect people from the malevolence of the dark side.[[6]](#cite_note-JoRMW4-6)

##### Showdown on Hissrich

:   "*My righteousness is anything but self-motivated. There is definitive* right *and there is* wrong*.* Good *and* evil*.*"
:   ―Mace Windu, to AD-W4[[40]](#cite_note-JoRMW5-40)

 [![Windu fought AD-W4 in single combat and ultimately destroyed the droid mercenary.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d1/MaceWinduVsADW4-JOTRMaceWindu5.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190118064921) [![Windu fought AD-W4 in single combat and ultimately destroyed the droid mercenary.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d1/MaceWinduVsADW4-JOTRMaceWindu5.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/285?cb=20190118064921)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d1/MaceWinduVsADW4-JOTRMaceWindu5.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190118064921) 

Windu fought AD-W4 in single combat and ultimately destroyed the droid mercenary.

 

While Fisto created a distraction by confronting the battle droids, his comrades executed their respective parts of the mission, with Mano infiltrating a [Separatist supply ship](/wiki/Dual_Hemisphere-Omni_Support_Vessel "Dual Hemisphere-Omni Support Vessel") and Windu challenging AD-W4 to single combat. As they fought, the droid mercenary attempted to bait Windu by accusing him of hypocrisy as well as secretly enjoying his newfound authority as a general in the Grand Army of the Republic. Although it briefly overpowered the Jedi Master, Windu ultimately prevailed, using both his Force powers and lightsaber to defeat AD-W4. He also rejected its claims against him, asserting that his virtues were influenced by altruism and the concept of right versus wrong.[[40]](#cite_note-JoRMW5-40)
AD-W4 was confident that its mission was a success in spite of the Jedi's efforts to prevent the Separatists from gaining a valuable energy source that could fuel their war effort against the Republic. However, Windu had anticipated the supply ship's purpose and instructed Mano to destroy it; the young Jedi Knight succeeded in her task—destroying the ship along with its flora samples—and moved to assist Fisto against the remaining droids in accordance with Windu's orders. Having failed in its mission, AD-W4 attempted to escape by disconnecting its head from its disabled body. The effort was in vain as Windu used the Force to cause the head to explode, destroying AD-W4 and ending the Separatist operation on Hissrich.[[40]](#cite_note-JoRMW5-40)

Returning to the Jedi Temple on Coruscant, Windu provided a report on the success of his team's mission to the High Council. The leaders of the Jedi Order decided to send a force of clone troopers to Hissrich, both to eliminate the remaining droids and provide aid to the planet's indigenous population. In addition to their plans for replanting and reconstruction on Hissrich, Yoda announced that they would study samples of the flora in order to learn more about its properties. The next item on their agenda was the trial of Prosset Dibs, who remained under arrest as a result of his conduct during the Hissrich operation. Dibs, who turned against his team and attacked Windu—a Jedi Master as well as a general in the Republic military—stood before the leaders of the Jedi Order accused of heresy and insubordination. He was ultimately found guilty on both charges, including [treason](/wiki/Treason "Treason"), but although Dibs expected to be put to death, Windu implored his colleagues to be merciful.[[40]](#cite_note-JoRMW5-40)

 [![After the events on Hissrich, Windu confided in Mano his concern for Dibs and the future of the Jedi Order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cd/MaceWinduAndRissaMano-JOTRMaceWindu5.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190118064700) [![After the events on Hissrich, Windu confided in Mano his concern for Dibs and the future of the Jedi Order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cd/MaceWinduAndRissaMano-JOTRMaceWindu5.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20190118064700)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cd/MaceWinduAndRissaMano-JOTRMaceWindu5.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190118064700) 

After the events on Hissrich, Windu confided in Mano his concern for Dibs and the future of the Jedi Order.

 

Windu, who harbored his own reservations against the Jedi's new military responsibilities,[[10]](#cite_note-JoRMW1-10) sympathized with Dibs' frustrations. In Windu's view, Dibs did not deserve to be faulted for feeling anger and confusion, both of which Windu regarded as valid emotions under the circumstances of war. As such, he believed that the Jedi had a duty to help rehabilitate the members of the Order who strayed from the light. Although Dibs continued to doubt Windu's sincerity, Windu requested for the prisoner to be placed on probation, confined to work in the [Jedi Archives](/wiki/Jedi_Archives "Jedi Archives") where he hoped Dibs would reevaluate his opinions. After the trial, Windu confessed to Mano his hope for reconciliation between Dibs and the Council, having sensed that the Order would need every Jedi as they faced their greatest challenge yet—a long war filled with trials and hardships. While he continued to yearn for a quick end to the fighting, Windu felt that it was not an attainable goal at the moment. The best that the Jedi Order could do, he believed, was to keep faith in the Force and stand in defense of not only the citizens of the Republic, but all peoples of the galaxy.[[40]](#cite_note-JoRMW5-40)

#### Rescue of Rotta

:   "*This is the opportunity we've been looking for. The Jedi must rescue Jabba's son.*"  
    "*Hmm… I don't like it—dealing with that criminal scum. This is a dark day for the Republic.*"
:   ―Sheev Palpatine and Mace Windu, on a potential alliance with Jabba Desilijic Tiure[[41]](#cite_note-TCW-film-41)

 [![During the Clone Wars, General Windu became a renowned warrior due to his forays onto the battlefield.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a0/Windu_Stak_Razor.png/revision/latest?cb=20121005161610) [![During the Clone Wars, General Windu became a renowned warrior due to his forays onto the battlefield.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a0/Windu_Stak_Razor.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/272?cb=20121005161610)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a0/Windu_Stak_Razor.png/revision/latest?cb=20121005161610) 

During the Clone Wars, General Windu became a renowned warrior due to his forays onto the battlefield.

 

As a senior member of the Jedi Council, Windu directed the Republic war effort from the Jedi Temple on Coruscant,[[4]](#cite_note-Databank-4) often conferring with Grand Master Yoda and Supreme Chancellor Palpatine on matters of strategy and diplomacy.[[41]](#cite_note-TCW-film-41) However, on occasion he also took to the field, commanding clone troopers and Jedi on several military campaigns[[4]](#cite_note-Databank-4) with Commander Ponds as his second-in-command.[[42]](#cite_note-Databank/Ponds-42) Windu's exploits on the battlefield served as a reminder of his reputation as a fierce warrior and champion of the Jedi Order.[[4]](#cite_note-Databank-4) He took command of the [187th Battalion](/wiki/187th_Battalion "187th Battalion")[[43]](#cite_note-The_Bad_Batch-43) and the elite [187th Legion](/wiki/187th_Legion "187th Legion").[[44]](#cite_note-Tank_Reveal-44)

During the early phase of the war, [Rotta](/wiki/Rotta "Rotta")—the [Huttlet](/wiki/Hutt "Hutt") son of [Jabba Desilijic Tiure](/wiki/Jabba_Desilijic_Tiure "Jabba Desilijic Tiure")—was "Huttnapped"[[45]](#cite_note-Databank/Rotta-45) by the Separatists,[[41]](#cite_note-TCW-film-41) who conspired to discredit the Jedi Knights in order to prevent a potential alliance between the Republic and the [Hutt Clan](/wiki/Hutt_Clan "Hutt Clan").[[45]](#cite_note-Databank/Rotta-45) In response to Rotta's abduction, Jabba issued a general distress call to anyone who was willing to rescue his son. Although Palpatine was quick to use this turn of events in the Republic's favor, Windu urged the chancellor to proceed with caution, believing there was more to the Huttlet's abduction than what was apparent. He also informed the chancellor that, because of the Separatist general [Grievous](/wiki/Grievous "Grievous"), Republic forces were stretched too thin to send a large number of Jedi on a rescue mission. Due to Palpatine's insistence that the Republic clone army needed to gain safe passage through the [Outer Rim](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Territories "Outer Rim Territories") [Hyperspace routes](/wiki/Hyperspace_route "Hyperspace route") in [Hutt Space](/wiki/Hutt_Space "Hutt Space"), Windu agreed to assign the mission to Obi-Wan Kenobi and Anakin Skywalker since both Jedi Knights were now available after [liberating](/wiki/Battle_of_Christophsis "Battle of Christophsis") the planet [Christophsis](/wiki/Christophsis "Christophsis") from Separatist occupation.[[41]](#cite_note-TCW-film-41)

 [![At the chancellor's request, Windu dispatched Kenobi and Skywalker on a mission to save Jabba's son.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/07/City_Plaza.png/revision/latest?cb=20121008214003) [![At the chancellor's request, Windu dispatched Kenobi and Skywalker on a mission to save Jabba's son.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/07/City_Plaza.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/264?cb=20121008214003)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/07/City_Plaza.png/revision/latest?cb=20121008214003) 

At the chancellor's request, Windu dispatched Kenobi and Skywalker on a mission to save Jabba's son.

 

Soon afterward Windu received a message from the [Advanced Recon Force Scout Troopers](/wiki/Advanced_Recon_Force_trooper "Advanced Recon Force trooper") who tracked Rotta's location to an [old monastery](/wiki/B%27omarr_Order_Monastery "B'omarr Order Monastery") on the planet [Teth](/wiki/Teth "Teth"). Due to the monastery's heavy fortification, Windu instructed the troopers to stand by and await Republic reinforcements. He then reassigned three of [Admiral](/wiki/Admiral "Admiral") [Wurtz](/wiki/Wurtz "Wurtz")'s [cruisers](/wiki/Cruiser "Cruiser") to the rescue operation. In spite of Count Dooku's plot to form an alliance between the Confederacy and the Hutt Clan, Rotta was ultimately redeemed from captivity by Anakin Skywalker and his new Padawan, [Ahsoka Tano](/wiki/Ahsoka_Tano "Ahsoka Tano"). The Separatists were [defeated](/wiki/Battle_of_Teth "Battle of Teth") on Teth and Jabba was made aware of Dooku's conspiracy, which in turn allowed the Republic to secure passage through the [Hyperspace](/wiki/Hyperspace "Hyperspace") lanes in Hutt territory.[[41]](#cite_note-TCW-film-41)

#### Liberation of Ryloth

:   "*General Windu! Perhaps we can come to a compromise.*"  
    "*Not when I hold all the cards.*"
