:   ―Wat Tambor and Mace Windu — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/40/IHoldAllTheCards-LoR.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250329115158)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:IHoldAllTheCards-LoR.flac "File:IHoldAllTheCards-LoR.flac"))[[46]](#cite_note-Liberty_on_Ryloth-46)

 [![Jedi Generals Windu and Kenobi played leading roles in the Ryloth campaign.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/70/Obi-Wan_and_Mace_Storm_Over_Ryloth.png/revision/latest?cb=20121003232220) [![Jedi Generals Windu and Kenobi played leading roles in the Ryloth campaign.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/70/Obi-Wan_and_Mace_Storm_Over_Ryloth.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/281?cb=20121003232220)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/70/Obi-Wan_and_Mace_Storm_Over_Ryloth.png/revision/latest?cb=20121003232220) 

Jedi Generals Windu and Kenobi played leading roles in the Ryloth campaign.

 

Following the Separatist invasion of the planet [Ryloth](/wiki/Ryloth "Ryloth"), the Jedi generals Windu, Kenobi and Yoda asked Senator [Bail Organa](/wiki/Bail_Prestor_Organa "Bail Prestor Organa") to negotiate with King [Katuunko](/wiki/Katuunko "Katuunko") of [Toydaria](/wiki/Toydaria "Toydaria"), hoping to gain his planet's support as a staging area for the delivery of relief supplies to the [Twi'lek](/wiki/Twi%27lek "Twi'lek") people.[[47]](#cite_note-Supply_lines-47) General Windu personally oversaw the [campaign](/wiki/Battle_of_Ryloth "Battle of Ryloth") to retake the Twi'lek homeworld. In response to the Republic's imminent counterattack, [Wat Tambor](/wiki/Wat_Tambor "Wat Tambor")—[foreman](/wiki/Foreman "Foreman") of the [Techno Union](/wiki/Techno_Union "Techno Union") and Separatist [emir](/wiki/Emir "Emir") of Ryloth—ordered the [Confederacy navy](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems_Navy "Confederacy of Independent Systems Navy") to form a blockade around the planet. As such, Windu entrusted Skywalker and Tano with the responsibility of breaking through the blockade in order to clear a path for the rest of the Republic invasion force. After some difficulty, Master and Padawan succeeded in their task, allowing Windu and Kenobi to commence with the landing of their ground forces on Ryloth.[[48]](#cite_note-Storm_Over_Ryloth-48)

In order to establish a foothold on Ryloth, Windu instructed Kenobi to lead a [detachment](/wiki/Ghost_Company "Ghost Company") of the [212th Attack Battalion](/wiki/212th_Attack_Battalion "212th Attack Battalion") on a mission to secure the landing area near the [city](/wiki/City "City") of [Nabat](/wiki/Nabat "Nabat"). On Tambor's orders, however, the Separatist battle droids used the local Twi'lek population as living shields to protect their [proton cannons](/wiki/Proton_cannon "Proton cannon"). Despite the danger that the [cannons](/wiki/Cannon "Cannon") posed to the [Republic Navy](/wiki/Republic_Navy "Republic Navy"), Windu informed Kenobi that freeing the hostages was a mission priority. After the success of Kenobi's assignment, Windu and his forces landed on the surface of Ryloth and proceeded with the final phase of the campaign—the liberation of the planetary capital city, [Lessu](/wiki/Lessu_City "Lessu City").[[49]](#cite_note-Innocents_of_Ryloth-49)

The liberation of Ryloth moved apace, but the march to the capital was perilous. After sustaining casualties and damage to his [All Terrain Tactical Enforcers](/wiki/All_Terrain_Tactical_Enforcer "All Terrain Tactical Enforcer"), Windu decided to enlist the aid of [Cham Syndulla](/wiki/Cham_Syndulla "Cham Syndulla"), the leader of the [local resistance](/wiki/Twi%27lek_Resistance "Twi'lek Resistance") against Separatist occupation. Syndulla was hesitant to align his cause with that of the Republic, fearing Ryloth would only trade one oppressing force for another. Yet the suffering of his people compelled him to communicate with Ryloth's own senator, [Orn Free Taa](/wiki/Orn_Free_Taa "Orn Free Taa").[[46]](#cite_note-Liberty_on_Ryloth-46) Windu long detested politics, but was nonetheless a capable diplomat.[[4]](#cite_note-Databank-4) His skills as a mediator enabled him to guide the corpulent politician and the freedom fighter to a compromise—Taa vowed that the clone army would withdraw from Ryloth after the remaining Separatists were driven away. In return, Syndulla promised to not use his popularity with the people to seize power from Ryloth's democratically-elected senator.[[46]](#cite_note-Liberty_on_Ryloth-46)

 [![After claiming victory on Ryloth, Windu attended a parade where the Twi'leks celebrated the liberation of their homeworld.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/21/Ryloth_parade.png/revision/latest?cb=20121005160221) [![After claiming victory on Ryloth, Windu attended a parade where the Twi'leks celebrated the liberation of their homeworld.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/21/Ryloth_parade.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/255?cb=20121005160221)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/21/Ryloth_parade.png/revision/latest?cb=20121005160221) 

After claiming victory on Ryloth, Windu attended a parade where the Twi'leks celebrated the liberation of their homeworld.

 

The combined forces of Republic clone troopers and Twi'lek freedom fighters laid siege to Lessu, which Tambor was in the process of evacuating, but not without confiscating much of Ryloth's wealth. The attack on the capital was led by both Syndulla and Windu, until the latter broke off from the main fighting in order to prevent Tambor's escape. As a result of the emir's delayed departure, Tambor was left stranded on Ryloth, allowing Windu to capture him at saber-point. Several Separatist [bombers](/wiki/Bomber "Bomber") made a last ditch attempt to bombard the capital, but their efforts ended in failure as Skywalker and Tano narrowly intercepted and destroyed the enemy [starfighters](/wiki/Starfighter "Starfighter") in their respective [Delta-7 Aethersprite-class light interceptors](/wiki/Delta-7_Aethersprite-class_light_interceptor "Delta-7 Aethersprite-class light interceptor").[[46]](#cite_note-Liberty_on_Ryloth-46)

With the liberation of Lessu and the capture of the [Skakoan](/wiki/Skakoan "Skakoan") emir, the campaign concluded in victory for both the Republic and Ryloth. Many Twi'leks gathered in the capital to celebrate their renewed liberty as clone troopers and freedom fighters marched through the city
in a triumphant parade. General Windu and Commander Ponds attended the event, as did Syndulla and Senator Taa.[[46]](#cite_note-Liberty_on_Ryloth-46)

#### Saving Neesha Tor

 [![Windu saved the life of a Twi'lek child named Neesha Tor.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/42/Mace_Windu_and_Neesha_Tor.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180825222704) [![Windu saved the life of a Twi'lek child named Neesha Tor.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/42/Mace_Windu_and_Neesha_Tor.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/159?cb=20180825222704)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/42/Mace_Windu_and_Neesha_Tor.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180825222704) 

Windu saved the life of a Twi'lek child named Neesha Tor.

 

:   "*I don't think so. I'm fairly confident I can get you back up there. But it's probably going to hurt.*"
:   ―Mace Windu, to Neesha Tor[[50]](#cite_note-A_Small_Push-50)

Sometime after Ryloth campaign, Windu was stationed on Ryloth. During this time, he saved [Neesha Tor](/wiki/Neesha_Tor "Neesha Tor")—a Twi'lek orphan who was treated like street trash. Using the Force, he pulled her to safety after she fell from a cliff.[[50]](#cite_note-A_Small_Push-50)

#### Holocron theft

:   "*You* will *take us to the holocron… And you will take us* now*.*"
:   ―Anakin Skywalker, Mace Windu and Obi-Wan Kenobi, using the Force to break Cad Bane's resolve[[51]](#cite_note-Children_of_the_Force-51)

 [![Todo 360 entered the communication center where he briefly encountered several Jedi Knights, including Yoda and Windu.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6b/Communication_center.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20091012001249) [![Todo 360 entered the communication center where he briefly encountered several Jedi Knights, including Yoda and Windu.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6b/Communication_center.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/256?cb=20091012001249)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6b/Communication_center.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20091012001249) 

Todo 360 entered the communication center where he briefly encountered several Jedi Knights, including Yoda and Windu.

 

In the aftermath of the [Confederate victory](/wiki/First_Battle_of_Felucia "First Battle of Felucia") on the planet [Felucia](/wiki/Felucia "Felucia"), Windu and the Jedi Council reprimanded Tano for her failure to immediately comply with the order to withdraw from the battle. As punishment, they temporarily reassigned her to serve as a guard in the Jedi Archives of the Temple. When Tano asked how long she would be on guard duty, Windu coldly responded by extending the punishment. Shortly afterward, Windu and Yoda discovered that the Temple had been infiltrated by thieves—unknown to the Jedi, Darth Sidious hired the bounty hunter [Cad Bane](/wiki/Cad_Bane "Cad Bane") for an assignment to steal one of the Order's [holocrons](/wiki/Holocron "Holocron"). As Kenobi and Skywalker hunted the intruders, Bane sacrificed his droid, [Todo 360](/wiki/Todo_360 "Todo 360"), by sending it to the [communication center](/wiki/Jedi_Temple_communication_center "Jedi Temple communication center") as a [bomb](/wiki/Bomb "Bomb"). Before the droid could detonate, Windu [Force pushed](/wiki/Force_push "Force push") Todo into the ventilation system where it exploded. The distraction worked to Bane's advantage, allowing the mercenary to escape the Temple with a holocron. However, Tano managed to apprehend his partner, [Cato Parasitti](/wiki/Cato_Parasitti "Cato Parasitti"), who revealed to Windu and the other Jedi that Bane's next target was [Bolla Ropal](/wiki/Bolla_Ropal "Bolla Ropal"), the keeper of the [Kyber memory crystal](/wiki/Kyber_memory_crystal "Kyber memory crystal"). Windu deduced the true nature of the theft—the holocron that Bane stole could be used to access the [crystal](/wiki/Crystal "Crystal")'s data, which contained the names and locations of all known Force-sensitive [children](/wiki/Youngling "Youngling") in the galaxy. With the future of the Jedi Order in jeopardy, the Council dispatched Kenobi to hunt Bane while Skywalker and Tano traveled to the [Devaron system](/wiki/Devaron_system "Devaron system") to find Ropal.[[52]](#cite_note-Holocron_Heist-52)

Skywalker and Tano were unsuccessful in their mission to thwart Bane's theft of the crystal. Knowing that the bounty hunter's next move was to abduct the Force-sensitive children, the Jedi switched to a new tactic—[meditation](/wiki/Meditation "Meditation"). Windu, Yoda, Kenobi and Skywalker searched through the Force, seeking to identify the children who were in immediate danger from Bane. The Force guided the Jedi to the planets [Rodia](/wiki/Rodia "Rodia") and Naboo. Kenobi failed to prevent the abduction of the [Rodian](/wiki/Rodian "Rodian") infant [Wee Dunn](/wiki/Wee_Dunn "Wee Dunn"), however the [Gungan](/wiki/Gungan "Gungan") child [Roo-Roo Page](/wiki/Roo-Roo_Page "Roo-Roo Page") was saved, and Bane was taken into Jedi custody by Skywalker and Tano. Windu personally conducted Bane's interrogation, although initially without success as he sensed that the mercenary's fear of his client outweighed his fear of the Jedi Order. At Tano's suggestion, Windu, Kenobi and Skywalker simultaneously performed the [mind trick](/wiki/Mind_trick "Mind trick") technique on Bane. Despite the possibility of permanently damaging Bane's mind in the process, the Jedi felt that he had given them no other recourse except to force his compliance for the sake of the Order's future. The experience proved too painful for Bane, who finally relented to the Jedi's demands.[[51]](#cite_note-Children_of_the_Force-51)

 [![Bane led Windu and Kenobi to the holocron and a trap.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/db/WinduKenobiBlackstall-COTF.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110917051946) [![Bane led Windu and Kenobi to the holocron and a trap.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/db/WinduKenobiBlackstall-COTF.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/264?cb=20110917051946)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/db/WinduKenobiBlackstall-COTF.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110917051946) 

Bane led Windu and Kenobi to the holocron and a trap.

 

Bane brought Windu, Kenobi, and Clone Commander [CC-2224](/wiki/Cody "Cody") to [Black Stall Station](/wiki/Black_Stall_Station "Black Stall Station") where the holocron was kept. The Jedi inadvertently trigger the station's defense [turrets](/wiki/Turret "Turret"), however, allowing Bane to leave the [space station](/wiki/Space_station "Space station") in an [escape pod](/wiki/Escape_pod "Escape pod") while Windu and Kenobi defended themselves. Both Jedi Masters ultimately survived the trap and escaped with the holocron just prior to the station's destruction. Simultaneously, Skywalker and Tano tracked the missing infants to the planet [Mustafar](/wiki/Mustafar "Mustafar") and were able to rescue them all before they could be used in the schemes of the [Dark Lord of the Sith](/wiki/Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith "Dark Lord of the Sith").[[51]](#cite_note-Children_of_the_Force-51)

#### Battle of Malastare

:   "*I have a bad feeling about this.*"
:   ―Mace Windu[[53]](#cite_note-The_Zillo_Beast-53)

 [![Seeking access to Malastarian fuel, the Republic dispatched an army led by Generals Windu and Skywalker to the Dug homeworld.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/af/Treaty_of_Malastare.png/revision/latest?cb=20120911231936) [![Seeking access to Malastarian fuel, the Republic dispatched an army led by Generals Windu and Skywalker to the Dug homeworld.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/af/Treaty_of_Malastare.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/272?cb=20120911231936)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/af/Treaty_of_Malastare.png/revision/latest?cb=20120911231936) 

Seeking access to Malastarian fuel, the Republic dispatched an army led by Generals Windu and Skywalker to the Dug homeworld.

 

When the Separatists invaded the planet [Malastare](/wiki/Malastare "Malastare"), homeworld of the [Dug](/wiki/Dug "Dug") [species](/wiki/Species "Species"), Windu again took to the field commanding Republic forces with the assistance of Commander Ponds and General Skywalker. Preventing the Separatist conquest of Malastare was not their only objective; the Republic sought to gain access to [Malastarian fuel](/wiki/Malastarian_fuel "Malastarian fuel"). [Doge](/wiki/Doge "Doge") [Nakha Urus](/wiki/Nakha_Urus "Nakha Urus"), leader of Malastare, agreed to sign a treaty of trade between the Republic and Malastare, provided that the Separatists were first driven off of Malastarian soil by Windu's forces. However, the Republic soon found itself heavily outnumbered upon confronting the Separatist invasion force on the open field of battle.[[53]](#cite_note-The_Zillo_Beast-53)

Despite this, the Republic had a backup plan—the [electro-proton bomb](/wiki/Electro-proton_bomb "Electro-proton bomb"), developed by the Republic scientist [Doctor](/wiki/Doctor "Doctor") [Sionver Boll](/wiki/Sionver_Boll "Sionver Boll"), was designed to neutralize a specific target: the Separatist battle droids. The doctor assured Windu and Chancellor Palpatine—who communicated with Republic forces via [hologram](/wiki/Hologram "Hologram")—that the bomb posed no threat to organic-based units, such as clone troopers and the Malastarian Dugs. The plan met with the Chancellor's approval, but did little to assuage Windu's concerns. Although the Jedi Master proposed to seek an alternative solution, the bomb's use was authorized by Palpatine and Urus. Upon detonation, the immediate blast incinerated the droids that were closest to the explosion. The subsequent discharge of [EMP radiation](/wiki/Electromagnetic_pulse "Electromagnetic pulse") caused the remaining the droids to shut down, along with every form of machinery within proximity of the overall blast.[[53]](#cite_note-The_Zillo_Beast-53)

 [![Windu and his forces discovered the Zillo Beast shortly after the Battle of Malastare.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f3/Hello_beastie.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110923031648) [![Windu and his forces discovered the Zillo Beast shortly after the Battle of Malastare.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f3/Hello_beastie.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/272?cb=20110923031648)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f3/Hello_beastie.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110923031648) 

Windu and his forces discovered the Zillo Beast shortly after the Battle of Malastare.

 

Though the experimental bomb succeeded in neutralizing the entire Separatist invasion force in one fell swoop, the surface began to collapse as a result of the explosion, creating a massive sinkhole that began at ground zero and expanded in every direction. A rescue operation soon commenced in order to search for the Republic troops who fell into the sinkhole. After losing communication with the rescue party, Windu and Ponds led a team to ascertain the fate of the survivors. Their investigation ultimately led them to discovering the [Zillo Beast](/wiki/Zillo_Beast "Zillo Beast")—an ancient creature native to Malastare, its species was long believed to be extinct by the Dug population. The beast, awoken by the bomb, chased after Windu and his troops, namely Ponds, [Trapper](/wiki/Trapper_(clone_trooper) "Trapper (clone trooper)"), and [Hawkeye](/wiki/Hawkeye "Hawkeye"), until Skywalker created a distraction by flying maneuvers around it in his Jedi starfighter.[[53]](#cite_note-The_Zillo_Beast-53)

After escaping from the sinkhole, Windu regrouped with Skywalker and Urus in order to develop a strategy to neutralize the Zillo Beast. The Malastarian doge was adamant that the creature (which he regarded as a "dangerous bloodthirsty monster") should be destroyed—a plan which Palpatine supported in order to ensure the Dugs' cooperation with the Republic's needs for Malastare's [fuel](/wiki/Fuel "Fuel"). Windu strongly objected on the ground of Jedi morality, however. Due to the possibility that the beast could be the last of its species, the Jedi Master was determined to preserve its life. His value for life ultimately conflicted with Urus' insistence on the creature's extermination. Urus went ahead with his plan upon discovering the harmful effects that Malastarian gas had on the Zillo Beast, prompting Windu to intercede in defense of the creature's life by threatening the doge with his lightsaber.[[53]](#cite_note-The_Zillo_Beast-53)

The situation was ultimately resolved when a group of Republic [RX-200 *Falchion*-class assault tanks](/wiki/RX-200_Falchion-class_assault_tank "RX-200 Falchion-class assault tank") concentrated their fire on the Zillo Beast and, as a result, incapacitated the creature. The Dugs believed that the beast was finally dead when in fact the [stun cannons](/wiki/Stun_cannon "Stun cannon") merely rendered it unconscious—long enough for Republic forces to transport the Zillo Beast to Coruscant for scientific research. Though the [Dug Council](/wiki/Dug_Council "Dug Council") formally ratified Malastare's treaty with the Republic,[[53]](#cite_note-The_Zillo_Beast-53) Windu made no effort to conceal his disapproval of Palpatine's decision to bring the dangerous beast to the galactic capital—a move that the Jedi Master regarded as folly on the Chancellor's part.[[4]](#cite_note-Databank-4)

#### Zillo Beast incident

:   "*With respect, Chancellor, I believe this creature could pose any number of dangers. Bringing it here to Coruscant is a mistake.*"
:   ―Mace Windu, to Sheev Palpatine[[54]](#cite_note-The_Zillo_Beast_Strikes_Back-54)

 [![Windu, the Jedi and their clone troopers were forced to destroy the Zillo Beast during its rampage on Coruscant.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/03/RexConfers-ZBSB.png/revision/latest?cb=20120912230505) [![Windu, the Jedi and their clone troopers were forced to destroy the Zillo Beast during its rampage on Coruscant.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/03/RexConfers-ZBSB.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/268?cb=20120912230505)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/03/RexConfers-ZBSB.png/revision/latest?cb=20120912230505) 

Windu, the Jedi and their clone troopers were forced to destroy the Zillo Beast during its rampage on Coruscant.

 

Windu returned to Coruscant with the sedated Zillo Beast in tow. As the clone army transported the beast to the [Republic Science and Technical Center](/wiki/Republic_Science_and_Technical_Center "Republic Science and Technical Center"), Windu again expressed his disapproval of Palpatine's decision to move a dangerous creature to the capital. By then, however, it was clear to him that the Chancellor would not listen to the Jedi Master's counsel on this matter. Palpatine claimed that the research conducted on the Zillo Beast would be beneficial to the Republic war effort, although his reassurance did little to alleviate Windu's concerns about the safety of Coruscant. At Kenobi's suggestion, the Jedi turned to Senator Padmé Amidala in the hopes that she would have more success in reasoning with the Chancellor.[[54]](#cite_note-The_Zillo_Beast_Strikes_Back-54)

Shortly after its arrival, however, the Zillo Beast [escaped](/wiki/Zillo_Beast_incident "Zillo Beast incident") from its confinement and proceeded to rampage through the cityscape of the galactic capital. Windu and the other Jedi mobilized Republic forces in order to prevent the beast from causing more damage and casualties on Coruscant. Palpatine, who had ordered the beast's destruction, was caught in its path while attempting to evacuate the [Senate Office Building](/wiki/Imperial_Executive_Building "Imperial Executive Building"). Windu and the Jedi consequently focused their efforts on saving the Chancellor's life, which ultimately led to the death of the Zillo Beast when Palpatine ordered the Republic [gunships](/wiki/Gunship "Gunship") to fire Malastarian [gas bombs](/wiki/Gas_bomb "Gas bomb") on it.[[54]](#cite_note-The_Zillo_Beast_Strikes_Back-54)

#### Senate conspiracy

:   "*We chose Senator Amidala because she and Clovis entered the Senate in the same year. They served on the same committees. They were… good friends.*"
:   ―Mace Windu, to Anakin Skywalker[[55]](#cite_note-Senate_Spy-55)

During the Clone Wars, Senator [Rush Clovis](/wiki/Rush_Clovis "Rush Clovis") of the planet [Scipio](/wiki/Scipio "Scipio") became a suspected traitor to the Republic. Due to the lack of proof, however, Windu and the Jedi Council instructed Skywalker to recruit Senator Amidala as a [spy](/wiki/Spy "Spy"), believing that their former relationship would enable the Naboo politician to gain the alleged traitor's confidence. Ultimately, the Council was right to be suspicious of Clovis as Amidala discovered proof that her colleague had secretly dealt with the Separatists on behalf of the [InterGalactic Banking Clan](/wiki/InterGalactic_Banking_Clan "InterGalactic Banking Clan") while pretending to be a Republic loyalist.[[55]](#cite_note-Senate_Spy-55)

#### Battle of Dantooine

:   "*I've just received a distress signal from our forces on Dantooine. Master Windu's defenses held, but at a great cost to his men. They need medical supplies immediately.*"
:   ―Ki-Adi-Mundi[[56]](#cite_note-Brain_Invaders-56)

On and off since the early weeks of the Clone War, Windu personally oversaw the [defense of Dantooine](/wiki/Defense_of_Dantooine "Defense of Dantooine") against oppositional forces that sought to wrest control of the planet from the Republic. The Jedi Master's forces prevented the fall of Dantooine to enemy control, but also sustained a large number of casualties in the process. After the battle Windu sent a distress signal, which Ki-Adi-Mundi received shortly after the Republic's [reconquest of Geonosis](/wiki/Second_Battle_of_Geonosis "Second Battle of Geonosis"), informing the Jedi of his victory while simultaneously requesting medical supplies for his injured soldiers.[[56]](#cite_note-Brain_Invaders-56)

#### Mission to Ridlay

 [![General Windu arrived on Ridlay with Commander Ponds and the clone troopers of Lightning Squadron.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ad/WinduLightningSquadron-SeparationAnxietyPartOne.png/revision/latest?cb=20240112061940) [![General Windu arrived on Ridlay with Commander Ponds and the clone troopers of Lightning Squadron.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ad/WinduLightningSquadron-SeparationAnxietyPartOne.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/260?cb=20240112061940)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ad/WinduLightningSquadron-SeparationAnxietyPartOne.png/revision/latest?cb=20240112061940) 

General Windu arrived on Ridlay with Commander Ponds and the clone troopers of Lightning Squadron.

 

Windu along with Commander Ponds and Lightning Squadron, were sent to investigate a communication blackout on [Ridlay](/wiki/Ridlay "Ridlay"). There, they found a village abandoned and only one person, [Agon](/wiki/Agon "Agon"). He claimed that ghost were coming toward the. Windu and the squadron then joined the villagers in their shelter. According to the villagers, the ghosts come every fifty years during Ridlay's eclipse for a celebration. However, the ghosts had driven them from their home. Windu believed there was something else with the ghosts and asked Agon to lead him to the [Ascension Well](/wiki/Ascension_Well "Ascension Well"). Windu and the squadron realized that ghosts were conflicted due to the presence of the Separatist being led by Dooku.[[57]](#cite_note-SAP1-57)

Windu fought Dooku until he [Force pushed](/wiki/Force_push "Force push") him. Dooku left their fight and ordered his battle droids to finish Windu and his forces off. Windu ordered Ponds and Lightning Squadron to retreat while he would finish off the droids. Windu then saved Agon from a ghost and was able to clear their minds of Dooku's poison. Windu and Agon watched as the ghosts returned to normal and left as the eclipse ended[[58]](#cite_note-SAP2-58)

#### Assassination attempt

:   "*Boba was on Geonosis when his father died. He watched as I killed him.*"  
    "*That would complicate things.*"  
    "*Indeed.*"
:   ―Mace Windu and Anakin Skywalker[[59]](#cite_note-R2_Come_Home-59)

 [![Trapped aboard the wreck of the Endurance, Windu and Skywalker were forced to wait for R2-D2 to return with help.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c3/WinduSkywalkerEndurance.png/revision/latest?cb=20120914035425) [![Trapped aboard the wreck of the Endurance, Windu and Skywalker were forced to wait for R2-D2 to return with help.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c3/WinduSkywalkerEndurance.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/263?cb=20120914035425)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c3/WinduSkywalkerEndurance.png/revision/latest?cb=20120914035425) 

Trapped aboard the wreck of the *Endurance*, Windu and Skywalker were forced to wait for R2-D2 to return with help.

 

As the war progressed, Boba Fett conspired to assassinate Windu out of vengeance for the death of father, the clone template Jango Fett. Aided by the bounty hunters [Aurra Sing](/wiki/Aurra_Sing "Aurra Sing"), [Bossk](/wiki/Bossk%27wassak%27Cradossk "Bossk'wassak'Cradossk"), and [Castas](/wiki/Castas "Castas"), Fett infiltrated a squad of clone [cadets](/wiki/Cadet "Cadet") during a tour of Windu's starship, the [*Venator*-class Star Destroyer](/wiki/Venator-class_Star_Destroyer "Venator-class Star Destroyer") *[Endurance](/wiki/Endurance "Endurance")*. Initially, Fett intended to kill Windu by placing an explosive device in the latter's quarters. However, the Jedi Master was called away mere [seconds](/wiki/Second "Second") before the bomb was triggered, resulting in the death of a clone trooper. As the *Endurance* crew searched the vessel for Windu's would-be assassin, the rogue clone amended his plan by sabotaging the [Star Destroyer](/wiki/Star_Destroyer "Star Destroyer")'s [reactor](/wiki/Reactor "Reactor") core, causing the [starship](/wiki/Starship "Starship") to crash into the surface of the planet [Vanqor](/wiki/Vanqor "Vanqor"). After escaping the doomed vessel, Windu and Skywalker's search for survivors led them to an escape pod that contained the cadets with the exception of Fett, whom Sing retrieved in *[Slave I](/wiki/Slave_I "Slave I")* prior to the Jedi's arrival.[[60]](#cite_note-Death_Trap-60)

In the aftermath of the destruction of the *Endurance*, Windu and Skywalker traveled to the crash site hoping to find survivors—including Admiral [Kilian](/wiki/Shoan_Kilian "Shoan Kilian") and CT-411, both of whom opted to remain with the ship as it went down. During the search, Windu chastised Skywalker for encouraging individuality in his droid, the [astromech unit](/wiki/Astromech_droid "Astromech droid") [R2-D2](/wiki/R2-D2 "R2-D2"). Before long, the Jedi generals discovered several dead clones along with signs that they had survived the crash only to be executed shortly after. On the bridge Skywalker discerned a [Mandalorian helmet](/wiki/Mandalorian_armor "Mandalorian armor") in the rubble. At that moment, Windu remembered both Jango and Boba Fett, leading the Jedi Master to realize that it was the latter who attempted to assassinate him. Although Windu was unable to prevent Skywalker from triggering the bomb within the helmet, he succeeded in saving the younger Jedi's life by pulling him away from the explosion through the Force. The blast caused even more damage to bridge, however, leaving both men trapped and injured under a large pile of debris. Unable to escape on their own, Skywalker instructed R2-D2 to relay their situation to the Jedi Temple. Windu, on the other hand, expressed little faith in the droid's ability to succeed.[[59]](#cite_note-R2_Come_Home-59)

As they lay trapped and waiting for the droid to return with help, Windu began to reflect on his actions at the Battle of Geonosis, particularly his victory over Jango Fett and how Boba witnessed his father's death at Windu's hand. Ultimately, Skywalker's droid returned with a rescue party—consisting of [Plo Koon](/wiki/Plo_Koon "Plo Koon"), Ahsoka Tano, and the clone troopers of [Wolfpack](/wiki/104th_Battalion "104th Battalion")—and managed to save both Jedi just prior to the full collapse of the *Endurance* bridge. Before returning to Coruscant, Windu praised R2-D2 for saving his life, much to Skywalker's surprise.[[59]](#cite_note-R2_Come_Home-59)

 [![Windu had no intention of seeking retribution for the attempt on his life&mdash;until he learned that Boba Fett's allies had taken hostages to force the Jedi's hand.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a8/HallsOfHealing-LT.png/revision/latest?cb=20120915024235) [![Windu had no intention of seeking retribution for the attempt on his life&mdash;until he learned that Boba Fett's allies had taken hostages to force the Jedi's hand.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a8/HallsOfHealing-LT.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/271?cb=20120915024235)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a8/HallsOfHealing-LT.png/revision/latest?cb=20120915024235) 

Windu had no intention of seeking retribution for the attempt on his life—until he learned that Boba Fett's allies had taken hostages to force the Jedi's hand.

 

After returning to the Republic capital, Windu and Skywalker recuperated at the Jedi Temple where they initially argued over their next course of action in light of Fett's attempt on their lives. Although Skywalker insisted that the Jedi should hunt the renegade clone and bring him to justice, Windu was content to let the matter go, preferring to not become entangled in a vendetta as Fett was against him. A transmission from Aurra Sing, who revealed the hostages she took from the *Endurance*, changed the Jedi Master's mind. Windu decided to confront Fett and his accomplices upon witnessing Sing's execution of CT-411, but due to his injuries he allowed Koon and Tano to go in his stead. Their mission was a success, resulting in Fett's arrest and the rescue of the remaining hostages. On Coruscant, Windu confronted Fett in person, who regretted his actions on the *Endurance*, but refused to forgive the Jedi for Jango's death.[[61]](#cite_note-Lethal_Trackdown-61) The unrepentant[[4]](#cite_note-Databank-4) clone was then sent to [prison](/wiki/Prison "Prison") by Windu.[[61]](#cite_note-Lethal_Trackdown-61)

### New threats and an ongoing war

#### Farr's funeral and the brother of Maul

Following Fett's arrest, Windu attended the [funeral](/wiki/Funeral_of_Onaconda_Farr "Funeral of Onaconda Farr") of the Rodian senator [Onaconda Farr](/wiki/Onaconda_Farr "Onaconda Farr"), who was assassinated by his personal [aide](/wiki/Aide "Aide"), [Lolo Purs](/wiki/Lolo_Purs "Lolo Purs").[[62]](#cite_note-SM-62)

Later in the war, the Jedi Council received a [holorecording](/wiki/Holorecorder "Holorecorder") of the [Devaron massacre](/wiki/Devaron_massacre "Devaron massacre"). Windu and Kenobi observed the footage which revealed the [Zabrak](/wiki/Zabrak "Zabrak") warrior [Savage Opress](/wiki/Savage_Opress "Savage Opress") whom Kenobi mistook for Darth Maul. Windu informed his colleague that the Zabrak in the recording was not the Sith Lord he fought on Naboo. He further explained that the Zabrak and Maul were [Dathomirians](/wiki/Dathomirian "Dathomirian") of [Dathomir](/wiki/Dathomir "Dathomir"), not [Iridonia](/wiki/Iridonia "Iridonia") as they previously believed in Maul's case.[[63]](#cite_note-WOTM-63)

#### Kidnapping of the Chancellor

:   "*Tell me about my target.*"  
    "*His name is Moralo Eval. Works directly for Count Dooku. Rumor is their plot will be hatched in three revolutions at the festival on Naboo.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi and Mace Windu[[64]](#cite_note-Deception-64)

 [![With Kenobi's aid, Windu and Skywalker intercepted the bounty hunters before they could escape with their valuable hostage.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5c/VictoryOnNaboo-Crisis.png/revision/latest?cb=20210228052401) [![With Kenobi's aid, Windu and Skywalker intercepted the bounty hunters before they could escape with their valuable hostage.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5c/VictoryOnNaboo-Crisis.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20210228052401)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5c/VictoryOnNaboo-Crisis.png/revision/latest?cb=20210228052401) 

With Kenobi's aid, Windu and Skywalker intercepted the bounty hunters before they could escape with their valuable hostage.

 

When rumors reached the Council that the bounty hunter [Moralo Eval](/wiki/Moralo_Eval "Moralo Eval") was planning to abduct Chancellor Palpatine despite his incarceration at the [Republic Judiciary Central Detention Center](/wiki/Republic_Judiciary_Central_Detention_Center "Republic Judiciary Central Detention Center"), Windu, Yoda, and Kenobi conceived a plan for Kenobi to infiltrate Eval's operation by impersonating the bounty hunter [Rako Hardeen](/wiki/Rako_Hardeen "Rako Hardeen"). Windu arranged for Skywalker to arrest Kenobi, posing as Hardeen, and have sent to prison. He was then informed that fellow bounty hunter Cad Bane was planning to free Eval.[[64]](#cite_note-Deception-64) Following Eval, Bane and Kenobi's [escape](/wiki/Riot_at_the_Republic_Judiciary_Central_Detention_Center "Riot at the Republic Judiciary Central Detention Center") from the detention center, Windu and Yoda rescinded the bounty to ensure that they would continue on their way to [Serenno](/wiki/Serenno "Serenno") where Count Dooku awaited their arrival.[[65]](#cite_note-Friends_and_Enemies-65)

While Kenobi continued to impersonate Hardeen, Windu accompanied the Supreme Chancellor to his homeworld of Naboo for the [Festival of Light](/wiki/Festival_of_Light "Festival of Light"). The bounty hunters [executed their plan](/wiki/Plan_to_kidnap_Chancellor_Palpatine "Plan to kidnap Chancellor Palpatine") during the ceremony, disabling the [ray shield](/wiki/Ray_shield "Ray shield") and kidnapping Palpatine. Through Kenobi's intervention, however, Windu and Skywalker were able to apprehend Bane and Eval before they could escape with their [prisoner](/wiki/Prisoner "Prisoner").[[66]](#cite_note-Crisis_on_Naboo-66)

#### Attack on the Temple

:   "*It is the Council's opinion that Padawan Ahsoka Tano has committed sedition against the Republic, and thus she will be expelled from the Jedi Order.*"
:   ―Mace Windu, pronouncing the Council's decision to expel Ahsoka Tano[[67]](#cite_note-The_Wrong_Jedi-67)

 [![Windu and the High Council summoned Padawan Tano to the Chamber of Judgment and found her guilty of treason.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/81/ChamberOfJudgement-TWJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20131029024016) [![Windu and the High Council summoned Padawan Tano to the Chamber of Judgment and found her guilty of treason.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/81/ChamberOfJudgement-TWJ.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/282?cb=20131029024016)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/81/ChamberOfJudgement-TWJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20131029024016) 

Windu and the High Council summoned Padawan Tano to the Chamber of Judgment and found her guilty of treason.

 

Following the a [terrorist](/wiki/Terrorist "Terrorist") [explosion](/wiki/Bombing_of_the_Jedi_Temple_hangar "Bombing of the Jedi Temple hangar") in a [hangar](/wiki/Hangar "Hangar") of the Jedi Temple, the Council recalled Skywalker and his apprentice to Coruscant. After briefing the two Jedi on the situation, Windu and Yoda assigned them to oversee the Jedi Order's internal investigation. In addition, they suspected that the attack was caused by a rogue Jedi. As neither Skywalker or Tano were present at the time of the bombing, Windu and the Grand Master considered them above suspicion and therefore suited to the task. Windu also assigned the analysis droid [Russo-ISC](/wiki/Russo-ISC "Russo-ISC") to the investigation, to work alongside Skywalker and Tano. During the investigation, Skywalker and Tano reported directly to Windu, who informed them that a swift conclusion to the case was imperative as rumors began to circulate within the Senate that the [military police](/wiki/Military_Police_(Galactic_Republic) "Military Police (Galactic Republic)") could become involved. With the arrest of [Letta Turmond](/wiki/Letta_Turmond "Letta Turmond"), Windu and Yoda concluded that the[[68]](#cite_note-Sabotage-68) radical[[69]](#cite_note-TurmondDB-69) [Coruscanti](/wiki/Coruscanti "Coruscanti") was the main culprit in the bombing of the Temple hangar. While there was no indication at the time of a Jedi's involvement, the incident served to fuel [anti-Jedi sentiment](/wiki/Anti-Jedi_sentiment "Anti-Jedi sentiment") among the Republic citizenry—an outcome that concerned Windu.[[68]](#cite_note-Sabotage-68)

In the aftermath of Turmond's arrest, Windu attended a [funeral ceremony](/wiki/Funeral_of_the_Jedi_Temple_bombing_victims "Funeral of the Jedi Temple bombing victims") to honor the six Jedi Knights who were killed in the hangar blast. Shortly thereafter, Skywalker's Padawan came under suspicion of being the true mastermind behind the bombing after Turmond was Force-choked to death in her presence.[[70]](#cite_note-TJWKTM-70) Admiral [Wilhuff Tarkin](/wiki/Wilhuff_Tarkin "Wilhuff Tarkin") contacted the Council and claimed that Tano had not only murdered Turmond, but also several clone troopers during her [escape](/wiki/Escape_from_the_Republic_military_base "Escape from the Republic military base") from the [Republic Center for Military Operations](/wiki/Imperial_Inspectorate_HQ "Imperial Inspectorate HQ"). The Council endeavored to apprehend the fugitive Padawan, although Windu was concerned by Yoda's decision to send Skywalker after his own apprentice, believing that his emotional connection to Tano would complicate the mission.[[71]](#cite_note-To_Catch_a_Jedi-71)

The hunt for Tano led to her [capture](/wiki/Capture_of_Ahsoka_Tano "Capture of Ahsoka Tano") and subsequent confinement in the Jedi Temple. As the Council debated on what to do with her, Tarkin contacted them on the Senate's behalf, imploring the Jedi leadership to expel Tano and surrender her to military custody.[[67]](#cite_note-The_Wrong_Jedi-67) Windu was troubled[[72]](#cite_note-Episode_Gallery-72) by the Council's options in the matter—to either stand by Tano, as Kenobi insisted; or remove her from the ranks of the Order as the Senate commanded.[[67]](#cite_note-The_Wrong_Jedi-67) Ultimately, Windu concurred with Tarkin on the grounds that failing to submit Tano for trial could be regarded as an act of opposition to the Senate.[[72]](#cite_note-Episode_Gallery-72) At Yoda's behest, the young Padawan was taken to the [Chamber of Judgment](/wiki/Chamber_of_Judgment "Chamber of Judgment"), where five members of the Council, including Windu, reviewed the charges against her and asked for her plea. Tano pleaded innocent and insisted that the Council was being deceived; but as she was unable to confirm the identity of the true perpetrator, Windu announced the Council's decision to revoke Tano's Jedi status and hand her over to the military custody of the Republic.[[67]](#cite_note-The_Wrong_Jedi-67)

 [![Although Windu proclaimed Tano a greater Jedi because of her ordeal, the former Padawan chose to walk away from the Jedi Order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cf/AhsokaLeavesTheOrder-TWJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20131029022852) [![Although Windu proclaimed Tano a greater Jedi because of her ordeal, the former Padawan chose to walk away from the Jedi Order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cf/AhsokaLeavesTheOrder-TWJ.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/272?cb=20131029022852)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cf/AhsokaLeavesTheOrder-TWJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20131029022852) 

Although Windu proclaimed Tano a greater Jedi because of her ordeal, the former Padawan chose to walk away from the Jedi Order.

 

After the expulsion was completed, Windu attended Tano's [military trial](/wiki/Trial_of_Ahsoka_Tano "Trial of Ahsoka Tano") alongside several other members of the Council. Before the verdict could be read, however, Skywalker burst in and revealed the real traitor, [Barriss Offee](/wiki/Barriss_Offee "Barriss Offee"), who confessed to the crimes that Tano had been accused of and scathingly claimed that the Jedi were the ones responsible for the Clone War.[[67]](#cite_note-The_Wrong_Jedi-67)

Due to this revelation, Windu and the Council attempted to make amends with Tano. In addition to a personal apology from Skywalker, Plo Koon informed Tano that she had the Council's most humble apologies.[[67]](#cite_note-The_Wrong_Jedi-67) [Saesee Tiin](/wiki/Saesee_Tiin "Saesee Tiin"), Mundi, and Windu all observed Tano's ordeal as a "[great trial](/wiki/Jedi_Trials "Jedi Trials")" in her training, and stated that she had become a greater Jedi[[72]](#cite_note-Episode_Gallery-72) than she would have been otherwise. But while Windu and his colleagues were prepared to accept her back into the Order with a promotion to the rank of Jedi Knight, Tano felt betrayed and refused the offer, instead choosing to leave the Temple to search for a new path.[[67]](#cite_note-The_Wrong_Jedi-67)

#### Mission to Bardotta

:   "*Your power is no match for my magics."  
    "Magic is only an illusion.*"
:   ―Talzin and Mace Windu[[73]](#cite_note-Disappeared_2-73)

 [![Windu fought Mother Talzin on Zardossa Stix.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5f/TalzinvsWindu.png/revision/latest?cb=20200226054619) [![Windu fought Mother Talzin on Zardossa Stix.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5f/TalzinvsWindu.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/271?cb=20200226054619)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5f/TalzinvsWindu.png/revision/latest?cb=20200226054619) 

Windu fought Mother Talzin on Zardossa Stix.

 

Windu later [accompanied](/wiki/Diplomatic_mission_to_Bardotta "Diplomatic mission to Bardotta") [Representative](/wiki/Junior_Representative "Junior Representative") [Jar Jar Binks](/wiki/Jar_Jar_Binks "Jar Jar Binks") to assist the [Bardottan](/wiki/Bardottan "Bardottan") Queen [Julia](/wiki/Julia "Julia") in finding the disappearing [Dagoyan Masters](/wiki/Dagoyan_Order "Dagoyan Order"). However, Windu's presence was not welcome by the Queen nor the Bardottans, due to a long-standing mistrust of the Jedi by the Dagoyans. Windu also sensed that the Force was out of balance on Bardotta. However, when the queen disappeared, Windu assisted the Bardottans and Binks in their search in the catacombs belonging to the [Frangawl Cult](/wiki/Frangawl_Cult "Frangawl Cult"). When Binks disappeared, Windu tracked him down and rescued Binks from being sacrificed. However, the Frangawl cult leader escaped with queen off-world. Binks promised the [Bahk-tov Council](/wiki/Bahk-tov_Council "Bahk-tov Council") that they would find the queen before the prophecy came to be.[[74]](#cite_note-Disappeared_1-74)

Windu learned from Binks that the Frangawl cult was extracting the living force from Dagoyan masters, and putting it into a sphere. He surmised that they would do same to Queen Julia. Windu then sensed the orb on [Zardossa Stix](/wiki/Zardossa_Stix "Zardossa Stix") where Windu sensed her in a city market square. Windu fought with several of the cultists and saved Binks from capture, then stunning one [Gundark](/wiki/Gundark "Gundark") and killing another. Windu questioned the Gundarks' trainer, who told them that the mysterious "[Great Mother](/wiki/Talzin "Talzin")" would deal with him. Windu and Binks took an [eopie](/wiki/Eopie "Eopie") and a [dalgo](/wiki/Dalgo "Dalgo") to help in their search, [traveling](/wiki/Mission_to_Zardossa_Stix "Mission to Zardossa Stix") to the Zardossan temple. However, Windu and Binks were then confronted by [stone guardians](/wiki/Stone_guardian "Stone guardian"), yet Windu was able to defeat them. He soon confronted the Great Mother, who revealed herself to be the [Nightsister](/wiki/Nightsisters "Nightsisters") Mother Talzin. With Binks' help, Windu was able to prevent Talzin from absorbing the sphere's power and watched as she disappeared.[[73]](#cite_note-Disappeared_2-73)

#### The truth about the clone army

:   "*Our enemy created an army for us.*"  
    "*If this was known, public confidence in the war effort, the Jedi, and the Republic would vanish. There would be* mass *chaos.*"
:   ―Yoda and Mace Windu[[75]](#cite_note-The_Lost_One-75)

 [![While investigating the death of Sifo-Dyas, the High Council discovered that the Sith were responsible for the creation of the clone army.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/39/SifoDyas_file.png/revision/latest?cb=20200224151650) [![While investigating the death of Sifo-Dyas, the High Council discovered that the Sith were responsible for the creation of the clone army.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/39/SifoDyas_file.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200224151650)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/39/SifoDyas_file.png/revision/latest?cb=20200224151650) 

While investigating the death of Sifo-Dyas, the High Council discovered that the Sith were responsible for the creation of the clone army.

 

Responding to a mysterious distress call, [Plo Koon](/wiki/Plo_Koon "Plo Koon") discovered a crashed Jedi shuttle, and found the lightsaber of Sifo-Dyas in the wreckage to the surprise of the High Council. Sifo-Dyas' lightsaber had been lost since his death a decade prior to the Clone Wars; Skywalker and Kenobi were sent to investigate, which led them to discover that Sifo-Dyas had, in fact, been murdered by [Pyke](/wiki/Pyke "Pyke") criminals rather than the native Felucians he had been sent to negotiate with, as the Council had previously assumed. Furthermore, they learned that the Pykes had been acting on orders from Count Dooku. A confrontation between Dooku and the Jedi on the [Oba Diah moon](/wiki/Oba_Diah_moon "Oba Diah moon") led the Order to discover that Dooku was the mysterious Tyranus who hired Jango Fett as the clone template, making him responsible for the clone army's creation.[[75]](#cite_note-The_Lost_One-75)

The High Council now knew that the Sith were involved in the development of clone troopers. However, they did not understand why their own enemy would provide them with the means to defend the Republic. Windu noted with caution that such a revelation could easily destroy public confidence in the Jedi, the Republic and the war effort. The conspiracy was therefore classified as confidential information; Yoda himself ordered his colleagues to not speak of their discovery to anyone, including Chancellor Palpatine. He also dismissed any doubts concerning the clone troopers, citing their valiant service and loyalty to the Jedi. Windu was uncertain about Yoda's decision, but the Grand Master assured him that it was the only feasible option available to the Jedi Order given the circumstances.[[75]](#cite_note-The_Lost_One-75)

#### Yoda's mission

:   "*There is great turmoil within Master Yoda.*"  
    "*Yes, we all sensed it.*"  
    "*For something to affect Yoda this deeply concerns me… We must keep an eye on our old friend.*"  
    "*The war has taxed all of us to our limit. I suppose we're just surprised Master Yoda has one.*"  
    "*I hope it's that simple, but I feel the shadow of something greater on our horizon.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi and Mace Windu, discussing their concern for Yoda[[76]](#cite_note-Voices-76)

 [![Windu and his fellow Council members became concerned about Yoda, who claimed to hear the voice of the deceased Qui-Gon Jinn.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b8/EpGuide611.png/revision/latest?cb=20200224044854) [![Windu and his fellow Council members became concerned about Yoda, who claimed to hear the voice of the deceased Qui-Gon Jinn.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b8/EpGuide611.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/262?cb=20200224044854)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b8/EpGuide611.png/revision/latest?cb=20200224044854) 

Windu and his fellow Council members became concerned about Yoda, who claimed to hear the voice of the deceased Qui-Gon Jinn.

 

Not long afterwards, Yoda started behaving strangely, becoming noticeably distracted and thoughtful during meetings. This surprised and concerned Windu, who sensed great turmoil within Yoda. He voiced his concerns to Obi-Wan Kenobi in a private discussion, and they resolved to keep a closer watch on their old friend. Later, a noticeably uncertain Yoda revealed that he had spoken with the deceased Qui-Gon Jinn. However, everything the Jedi knew about the Force suggested that the ability to retain one's individuality after death was impossible, so the reactions from the Council ranged from concern to skepticism and suspicion. Though they meditated with Yoda for a whole day, they were unable to sense anything. After the failed meditation, Ki-Adi-Mundi suggested that what Yoda was sensing could be a deception by the Sith. Kenobi refused to believe that Yoda could be susceptible to such manipulation, but Windu replied that, even as wise and old as he was, Yoda was not beyond the corruption of the dark side. The ancient Jedi master agreed and submitted himself to medical examination.[[76]](#cite_note-Voices-76)

Windu, Kenobi and Mundi were told by [Rig Nema](/wiki/Rig_Nema "Rig Nema") that Yoda was in perfect mental health, even though he was approaching the nine hundredth year of his life. Mundi, who was particularly skeptical of Yoda's claims, suggested the Dark Lord of the Sith could be using Yoda's connection to Dooku to manipulate him, but Kenobi vehemently rejected the idea, saying they all had been apprenticed to Yoda at one point or another. Before the discussion could go on, Nema suggested a deprivation ritual for Yoda to reach the source of the voice. During the procedure, Kenobi, Skywalker, Mundi, and Plo Koon watched over the small Jedi. Yoda managed to hear Jinn's instruction to go to the [Dagobah system](/wiki/Dagobah_system "Dagobah system") before Kenobi noticed his vital signs were dropping too low and stopped the test.[[76]](#cite_note-Voices-76)

 [![Though clouded by the dark side, Yoda beheld a vision of the fate of Mace Windu and the other members of the Jedi Order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/49/Yoda_vision_of_the_Jedi_Purge.png/revision/latest?cb=20200224055921) [![Though clouded by the dark side, Yoda beheld a vision of the fate of Mace Windu and the other members of the Jedi Order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/49/Yoda_vision_of_the_Jedi_Purge.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200224055921)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/49/Yoda_vision_of_the_Jedi_Purge.png/revision/latest?cb=20200224055921) 

Though clouded by the dark side, Yoda beheld a vision of the fate of Mace Windu and the other members of the Jedi Order.

 

When Windu asked about the procedure, Kenobi told him that Yoda was sure he had contacted the dead. Mundi asserted that Yoda's claim was impossible, and again voiced his suspicion that Yoda was under attack by the Sith. More concerned than ever, Windu ordered temple guards to monitor all of Yoda's moves. However, the diminutive Jedi Master soon managed to escape with Skywalker's help and R2-D2's company, willing to go on a journey that would take him to the mysterious world of [Dagobah](/wiki/Dagobah "Dagobah") as well as the ancient Sith homeworld of [Moraband](/wiki/Moraband "Moraband"). Immediately after Yoda's escape,[[76]](#cite_note-Voices-76) a furious[[77]](#cite_note-Voices_Episode_Gallery-77) Windu confronted Skywalker, but the younger Jedi countered that, for once, none of what had occurred had been his idea. After arriving on Dagobah, Yoda was led to the [Cave of Evil](/wiki/Cave_of_Evil "Cave of Evil") by the disembodied voice of Jinn. The [cave](/wiki/Cave "Cave") was strong with the dark side, causing Yoda to foresee clouded visions of the deaths of Windu and other members of the Jedi Order, followed by the ascent of the Sith Lord Darth Sidious.[[76]](#cite_note-Voices-76)

On Yoda's return to Coruscant, Windu and Kenobi greeted him, and Windu stated that the High Council was eager to hear Yoda's report, but the old Jedi master claimed that there was not much to discuss. When Windu asked him if his journey had given him insight on how to win the war, Yoda told them that he was no longer certain that the Jedi could win the Clone Wars but that, through hope and perseverance, the Jedi would ultimately triumph over the Sith.[[78]](#cite_note-Sacrifice-78)

#### The Dooku assassination attempt

:   "*Isn't protecting the innocent the very definition of what it means to be a Jedi? We are failing the Republic and its citizens. We must stop this—*now*.*"
:   ―Mace Windu, to the Jedi High Council[[79]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-79)

 [![Distressed by the growing number of casualties, the High Council sent Quinlan Vos and Asajj Ventress to assassinate Count Dooku.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/03/Dark_Disciple_Cover_Detail.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20151124230540) [![Distressed by the growing number of casualties, the High Council sent Quinlan Vos and Asajj Ventress to assassinate Count Dooku.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/03/Dark_Disciple_Cover_Detail.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/246?cb=20151124230540)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/03/Dark_Disciple_Cover_Detail.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20151124230540) 

Distressed by the growing number of casualties, the High Council sent Quinlan Vos and Asajj Ventress to assassinate Count Dooku.

 

Upon witnessing a devastating Separatist [attack](/wiki/Atrocity_on_Mahranee "Atrocity on Mahranee") on [Mahranee](/wiki/Mahranee "Mahranee"), as well as the killing of many [Mahran](/wiki/Mahran "Mahran") refugees, Mace Windu urged the Jedi Council to consider his proposal to assassinate Count Dooku. At first, Obi-Wan Kenobi and Yoda opposed this course action, believing that such measures could draw them closer to the dark side, but Windu countered their argument by reminding them of Dooku's significance to the Separatist war effort. He also warned that unless the Jedi learned to adapt, the war and its devastating effect on the galaxy could continue indefinitely. Anakin Skywalker, who had been invited by Kenobi to attend the Council's meeting, agreed with Windu.[[79]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-79)

Windu and Skywalker also pointed to the war's growing number of civilian casualties, noting that many more lives would be lost as long as the conflict continued. Having considered Windu's words, including his stance on the Jedi Order's responsibility to protect the innocent, the Republic and its citizens, the Council agreed to sanction the plan. At Kenobi's suggestion, they assigned the mission to Jedi Master [Quinlan Vos](/wiki/Quinlan_Vos "Quinlan Vos"), due to his experience with covert operations. Vos, in turn recruited Dooku's former apprentice, [Asajj Ventress](/wiki/Asajj_Ventress "Asajj Ventress"). However, after becoming lovers Ventress convinced Vos to train in the ways of the dark side in order to defeat Dooku.[[79]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-79)

The mission ended in failure, as Dooku was able to defeat both Force-sensitive assassins, resulting in Vos' [capture](/wiki/Mission_to_Raxus_Secundus "Mission to Raxus Secundus") on Raxus Secundus. When Ventress reported directly to the Jedi Council, Windu greeted her with an arrest warrant, but was persuaded by Kenobi and Yoda to hear her account of the mission. He was particularly displeased to learn that Ventress exposed Vos to the dark side, but the former Separatist retorted by reminding Windu that he and the Council had assigned Vos the mission in the first place. When the Council decided to [rescue](/wiki/Rescue_of_Quinlan_Vos "Rescue of Quinlan Vos") Vos, Windu became exasperated by their decision to send Ventress on the mission, but reluctantly agreed to follow Yoda's plan.[[79]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-79)

Although the rescue mission was a success, Windu and the Council soon grew suspicious of Vos' allegiance. After definitively concluding that Vos had secretly joined Dooku, and having considered the repercussions that could result from the fall of a Jedi Master of Vos' stature, Windu proposed that the Council consider the possibility of executing him as punishment for treason. Most of the Council was supportive of this idea, given the Order's history with other Jedi who turned to the dark side such as Barriss Offee, Pong Krell, and especially Dooku, but Kenobi persuaded them to give Vos the chance to reaffirm his commitment to the Jedi and the Republic by making another attempt on the Count's life. In the event that Vos failed to assassinate Dooku, Kenobi and Skywalker were under orders from Windu to execute Vos.[[79]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-79)

Following the [second battle of Christophsis](/wiki/Second_battle_of_Christophsis "Second battle of Christophsis"), the Council once again met to discuss the fate of Quinlan Vos, who renounced the dark side after Ventress[[79]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-79) seemingly[[80]](#cite_note-TBB_article-80) died while defending him from Dooku. At the same time, Windu spoke well of Ventress, commending her decision to sacrifice her life for another. Kenobi, however, felt that he and the Council did not understand the true depths of her sacrifice. Despite their disagreement on the use of assassination, as well as the circumstances surrounding Vos' temporary turn to the dark side, the Council agreed to give him the chance to regain their trust by atoning for his actions.[[79]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-79)

#### Tracking Maul

:   "*Stand down in the name of the Republic… This has gone far enough, Dooku.*"
:   ―Mace Windu, to Maul and Count Dooku[[81]](#cite_note-Son_of_Dathomir_3-81)

 [![Windu oversaw the hunt for Maul, believing that his capture could help to end the Clone Wars.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/26/Mace_Windu_Ord_Mantell.png/revision/latest?cb=20140716201831) [![Windu oversaw the hunt for Maul, believing that his capture could help to end the Clone Wars.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/26/Mace_Windu_Ord_Mantell.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/249?cb=20140716201831)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/26/Mace_Windu_Ord_Mantell.png/revision/latest?cb=20140716201831) 

Windu oversaw the hunt for Maul, believing that his capture could help to end the Clone Wars.

 

In the aftermath of a [battle](/wiki/Battle_on_Ord_Mantell "Battle on Ord Mantell") between the Separatists and [Shadow Collective](/wiki/Shadow_Collective "Shadow Collective"), Chancellor Palpatine informed Windu that Count Dooku and Maul were seen near [Ord Mantell](/wiki/Ord_Mantell "Ord Mantell"). Acting on the Chancellor's information, Windu led a force of clone troopers—alongside fellow generals Kenobi, [Tiplee](/wiki/Tiplee "Tiplee"), and [Aayla Secura](/wiki/Aayla_Secura "Aayla Secura")—to the battle site in the hopes of ending the war by capturing both Sith. After investigating the area, they found the [helmet](/wiki/Armor "Armor") of a [Mandalorian super commando](/wiki/Mandalorian_super_commando "Mandalorian super commando") which led Windu to confirm that the alliance between Prime Minister [Almec](/wiki/Almec "Almec")'s government and the criminal underworld remained intact. Following this, the Jedi tracked Maul to [Vizsla Keep 09](/wiki/Vizsla_Keep_09 "Vizsla Keep 09") and proceeded with a direct [assault](/wiki/Assault_on_Vizsla_Keep_09 "Assault on Vizsla Keep 09") on the [Mandalorian](/wiki/Mandalorian "Mandalorian") outpost. During the attack, Windu and Secura dueled with Maul while Dooku fought Kenobi and Tiplee, who was ultimately slain by the former Jedi Master.[[81]](#cite_note-Son_of_Dathomir_3-81)

Despite their efforts, both Sith Lords were able to escape from the outpost with the support of Maul's commandos. In the aftermath of the battle, Windu reported to the Chancellor and conveyed his suspicion that Dooku and Maul were master and apprentice—a theory which led him to believe that Dooku may have been the second Sith that the Jedi had been searching for since the Naboo crisis.[[81]](#cite_note-Son_of_Dathomir_3-81)

#### Anaxes

:   "*My name is General Mace Windu of the Jedi Order. At this point of the Clone War, I have dismantled and destroyed over 100,000 of you type one battle droids. I'm giving you an opportunity to peacefully lay down your weapons, so that you may be reprogrammed to serve a better purpose than spreading the mindless violence and chaos which you have inflicted upon the galaxy.*"
:   ―Mace Windu, to an army of battle droids[[82]](#cite_note-Unfinished_Business-82)

 [![Windu led his clone troopers into battle on Anaxes.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/25/187th-Anaxes.png/revision/latest?cb=20241018044312) [![Windu led his clone troopers into battle on Anaxes.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/25/187th-Anaxes.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/268?cb=20241018044312)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/25/187th-Anaxes.png/revision/latest?cb=20241018044312) 

Windu led his clone troopers into battle on Anaxes.

 

Later in the war, Windu led the 187th Battalion along with Skywalker and the [501st Legion](/wiki/501st_Legion "501st Legion") to the planet [Anaxes](/wiki/Anaxes "Anaxes") which was under [attack](/wiki/Battle_of_Anaxes "Battle of Anaxes") by Admiral [Trench](/wiki/Trench "Trench"). The Separatists had gained the upper hand in the battle despite weeks of battle. At the Republic base, Windu conferred with Skywalker after the droids had over run their main production unit which indicated them losing. 501st [Legion](/wiki/Legion "Legion") [Captain](/wiki/Captain "Captain") [Rex](/wiki/Rex "Rex") and 212th Attack [Battalion](/wiki/Battalion "Battalion") Commander Cody arrived, and Rex shared his theory that the droids had learned his personal strategies. Windu allowed them to take a small squad of troopers to go behind enemy lines to infiltrate the [Cyber Center](/wiki/Cyber_Center "Cyber Center") to learn more.[[43]](#cite_note-The_Bad_Batch-43)

Unknown to Windu and Skywalker, as Rex felt they may believe he was crazy for thinking it, Rex also felt that [ARC trooper](/wiki/Advanced_Recon_Commando "Advanced Recon Commando") [CT-1409](/wiki/Echo "Echo") "Echo," who was thought to have been killed during the [Battle of Lola Sayu](/wiki/Battle_of_Lola_Sayu "Battle of Lola Sayu"), was still alive, as the strategies used by himself and the Separatists were battle plans Rex had made with the trooper. Ultimately, however, Rex was correct,[[43]](#cite_note-The_Bad_Batch-43) and Echo was [rescued](/wiki/Mission_to_Skako_Minor_(Clone_Wars) "Mission to Skako Minor (Clone Wars)") from [Skako Minor](/wiki/Skako_Minor "Skako Minor"). Following this, Windu debriefed Kenobi, Skywalker, Rex and Jesse on his plan to retake the [Separatist assembly complex](/wiki/Anaxes_assembly_complex "Anaxes assembly complex") by air, when Echo posed his plan to be escorted by the Bad Batch into Trench's new comm vault on a dreadnought on the planet's orbit and plug himself to feed the Separatist's strategic movements. Windu along with Kenobi, lead the assault along with the 501st Legion, 91st Mobile Reconnaissance Corps and 212th Attack Battalion attacking the complex. The battle ended with all other fronts falling to the Republic, Trench initiated a countdown for an explosion that could destroy most of Anaxes. Windu assisted with deactivating the bomb and managed to save Anaxes. Following the victory, Windu commended Rex, Clone Force 99 and Echo for their efforts during the battle, but Echo and the commandos left before the Republic's [medal](/wiki/Unidentified_medal_(Battle_of_Anaxes) "Unidentified medal (Battle of Anaxes)") ceremony.[[82]](#cite_note-Unfinished_Business-82)

### Last days of the war

Windu kept a close eye on the recovery of Billaba, following her disastrous defeat at the [Battle of Haruun Kal](/wiki/Battle_of_Haruun_Kal "Battle of Haruun Kal"). When she finally emerged from a [bacta tank](/wiki/Bacta_tank "Bacta tank"), Windu gently chided her for "being glib" and expressed to Yoda his concerns about her mental health, suggesting a full fitness assessment. Windu, along with Kenobi, then observed the initiate trials of [Caleb Dume](/wiki/Kanan_Jarrus "Kanan Jarrus"), [Tai Uzuma](/wiki/Tai_Uzuma "Tai Uzuma"), and [Sammo Quid](/wiki/Sammo_Quid "Sammo Quid") as well as Billaba's assessments. Windu congratulated her on her performance, as the Council accepted her back.[[83]](#cite_note-Kanan_7-83)

Shortly after, Windu and Kenobi showed up to provide aid to Billaba and Dume, following an [attack on the Temple](/wiki/Bombing_at_the_Jedi_Temple "Bombing at the Jedi Temple").[[84]](#cite_note-Kanan_8-84) He also assigned Billaba and her [battalion](/wiki/Depa_Billaba%27s_second_battalion "Depa Billaba's second battalion") a new mission to [Mygeeto](/wiki/Mygeeto "Mygeeto").[[85]](#cite_note-Kanan_9-85)

#### Shattered trust

:   "*I sense a plot to destroy the Jedi. The dark side of the Force surrounds the Chancellor.*"
:   ―Mace Windu, expressing his concern for the future of the Order[[33]](#cite_note-ROTS-33)

 [![Windu confronted Palpatine upon discovering his true identity as Darth Sidious, the Sith Lord responsible for the Clone Wars.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b9/DuelonCoruscant.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111028234030) [![Windu confronted Palpatine upon discovering his true identity as Darth Sidious, the Sith Lord responsible for the Clone Wars.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b9/DuelonCoruscant.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/254?cb=20111028234030)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b9/DuelonCoruscant.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111028234030) 

Windu confronted Palpatine upon discovering his true identity as Darth Sidious, the Sith Lord responsible for the Clone Wars.

 

Following the [Battle of Coruscant](/wiki/Battle_of_Coruscant "Battle of Coruscant"),[[33]](#cite_note-ROTS-33) Windu was disturbed by Chancellor Palpatine's decision to appoint Anakin Skywalker as his representative on the Jedi High Council.[[4]](#cite_note-Databank-4) Though the Council obliged the Chancellor, hoping to use the young Jedi as a spy against him,[[33]](#cite_note-ROTS-33) Windu warned his colleagues that it was dangerous to pair Skywalker with Palpatine.[[4]](#cite_note-Databank-4) Skywalker reacted with anger to the Council's decision to withhold the status of Jedi Master from him, but was quickly put in his place by Windu.[[86]](#cite_note-Databank_BG-86) At this time, the Council grew doubtful that Palpatine would surrender his wartime powers.[[33]](#cite_note-ROTS-33) As such, Windu agreed that the Chancellor would have to be removed by force and further added that the Council would have to take control of the Senate[[4]](#cite_note-Databank-4) in order to maintain peace during the transitional period.[[33]](#cite_note-ROTS-33) Shortly after, Ahsoka Tano, alongside the recently-promoted Commander Rex, reported a successful capture of Maul during the [Siege of Mandalore](/wiki/Siege_of_Mandalore "Siege of Mandalore"). Tano requested to speak with Skywalker, but was refused due to Skywalker's task with the Chancellor. Upon learning that Kenobi had located and engaged General Grievous, Tano believed that the war could be over soon, but Windu noted that the war's conclusion depended on Palpatine. When Tano questioned what he meant, Windu declined to discuss matters further with a citizen, stating that it was the business of the High Council. Tano responded that she understood, and Windu gave Tano a final nod before ending his transmission.[[87]](#cite_note-Shattered-87)

#### Duel with Darth Sidious

:   "*I am going to end this once and for all!*"  
    "*You can't! He must stand trial!*"  
    "*He has control of the Senate and the courts! He's too dangerous to be left alive!*"
:   ―Mace Windu and Anakin Skywalker, before the latter betrays the former[[33]](#cite_note-ROTS-33)

With the death of General Grievous during the [Battle of](/wiki/Battle_of_Utapau "Battle of Utapau") [Utapau](/wiki/Utapau "Utapau"), Windu was determined to see the Senate restored to its former position prior to the Clone Wars.[[33]](#cite_note-ROTS-33) By then, however, Skywalker revealed to Windu that Sheev Palpatine was in fact Darth Sidious, the mastermind behind the war and the second Sith that the Jedi had been searching for since the Naboo crisis. Realizing the Jedi had been deceived and knowing that the future of the Jedi Order was in grave danger, Windu and three other Jedi Masters—[Agen Kolar](/wiki/Agen_Kolar "Agen Kolar"), Tiin, and Fisto—raced to Palpatine's office and attempted to arrest the Supreme Chancellor.[[4]](#cite_note-Databank-4) Their [confrontation](/wiki/Duel_in_Palpatine%27s_office "Duel in Palpatine's office") led to a [lightsaber duel](/wiki/Lightsaber_duel "Lightsaber duel") in which Sidious killed the latter three with ease.[[33]](#cite_note-ROTS-33)

 [![Windu was electrocuted by Darth Sidious before being defenestrated](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a5/Windu-lightning-effects-2.png/revision/latest?cb=20130218041925) [![Windu was electrocuted by Darth Sidious before being defenestrated](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a5/Windu-lightning-effects-2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130218041925)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a5/Windu-lightning-effects-2.png/revision/latest?cb=20130218041925) 

Windu was electrocuted by Darth Sidious before being defenestrated

 

Despite the loss of his comrades, Windu continued to fight and ultimately prevailed in the duel,[[86]](#cite_note-Databank_BG-86) disarming the Sith Lord in the process.[[33]](#cite_note-ROTS-33) Skywalker, who had followed Windu despite the latter's orders to remain in the Temple, beseeched the Jedi Master to spare the Chancellor's life, believing Sidious had the power to save Padmé Amidala from death.[[4]](#cite_note-Databank-4) Windu, whose original goal was to put the Chancellor on trial, concluded that Sidious was too dangerous to be left alive due to his control over the Senate and the courts. But before Windu could deliver the killing strike, Skywalker betrayed Windu by severing his right hand,[[33]](#cite_note-ROTS-33) enabling Sidious to unleash a torrent of [Force lightning](/wiki/Force_lightning "Force lightning") that sent the Jedi Order's great champion plummeting to his death.[[4]](#cite_note-Databank-4)

### Legacy

#### Fall of the Jedi

:   "*Every single Jedi, including your friend, Obi-Wan Kenobi, is now an enemy of the Republic.*"  
    "*I understand.*"
:   ―Darth Sidious and Darth Vader[[33]](#cite_note-ROTS-33)

While Skywalker was horrified over causing Windu's death, he realized that there was no turning back, which caused him to turn to the dark side and become Sidious' apprentice, therefore betraying the Jedi. Sidious used Windu's attempt on his life to brand the Jedi as [traitors](/wiki/Treason "Treason"). After ordering Skywalker, who became the Sith Lord Darth Vader, to lead the [attack on the Jedi Temple](/wiki/Operation:_Knightfall "Operation: Knightfall"), [wipe out the separatists and shut down the battle droids](/wiki/Mission_to_Mustafar "Mission to Mustafar"),[[33]](#cite_note-ROTS-33) Sidious [brainwashed](/wiki/Behavioral_modification_biochip "Behavioral modification biochip") most of the clone troopers[[88]](#cite_note-Journeys_Beginnings-88) into turning on the Jedi by ordering them to execute [Order 66](/wiki/Order_66 "Order 66"), ultimately leading to the [downfall and near destruction](/wiki/Great_Jedi_Purge "Great Jedi Purge") of the Jedi Order.[[33]](#cite_note-ROTS-33)

#### Age of the Empire

:   "*Master Windu spoke highly of your heroics at the Battle of Lessu.*"  
    "*Ah. Mace Windu. Outnumbered 100 to one, we charged across Lessu's energy bridge to certain doom. We would not be stopped. They named that attack in songs, 'The Hammer of Ryloth.'*"
:   ―[Kanan Jarrus](/wiki/Kanan_Jarrus "Kanan Jarrus") and Cham Syndulla[[89]](#cite_note-SWR:Homecoming-89)

 [![Despite Imperial propaganda, the Twi'leks regarded Windu as a hero for his part in the liberation of Ryloth.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/51/Windu_ARF.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110921013922) [![Despite Imperial propaganda, the Twi'leks regarded Windu as a hero for his part in the liberation of Ryloth.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/51/Windu_ARF.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20110921013922)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/51/Windu_ARF.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110921013922) 

Despite Imperial propaganda, the Twi'leks regarded Windu as a hero for his part in the liberation of Ryloth.

 

Shortly after the [Battle of Fortress Vader](/wiki/Battle_of_Fortress_Vader "Battle of Fortress Vader"), Vader entered a [portal](/wiki/Portal "Portal") constructed by [Darth Momin](/wiki/Darth_Momin "Darth Momin") to resurrect his wife, Padmé Amidala. While walking through visions, he encountered Windu along with many Jedi with their lightsabers ready to battle him. However, Vader destroyed all of the illusions, cutting off Windu's hand and then slashing his throat as the words "Let the past die" resounded in his mind.[[90]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_25-90)

The name of Mace Windu was later reviled by those who believed the line of the [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire"). The Empire taught in their history books that Windu was the leader of a "criminal gang" that interfered with a legal execution taking place on Geonosis, thus sparking the Clone Wars.[[91]](#cite_note-loststars-91) However, Windu's reputation was not completely tarnished by Imperial [propaganda](/wiki/Propaganda "Propaganda").
