During the [Imperial Era](/wiki/Imperial_Era "Imperial Era"), the people of Ryloth still remembered his exploits and heroic deeds in the Battle of Lessu, and ultimately immortalized his name along with Cham Syndulla's through songs dedicated to their victory.[[89]](#cite_note-SWR:Homecoming-89) He would be remembered as "[The Hammer of Ryloth](/wiki/The_Hammer_of_Ryloth "The Hammer of Ryloth"),"[[92]](#cite_note-GoH_news-92) a name also gifted to Syndulla[[93]](#cite_note-Dawn-93) and their storming of Lessu.[[89]](#cite_note-SWR:Homecoming-89)

Windu was also remembered by Obi-Wan Kenobi,[[94]](#cite_note-There_is_Always_Another-94) his colleague on the High Council,[[33]](#cite_note-ROTS-33) who [ascended](/wiki/Rescue_of_Princess_Leia "Rescue of Princess Leia") to the [Cosmic Force](/wiki/Cosmic_Force "Cosmic Force") as a [Force spirit](/wiki/Force_spirit "Force spirit") during the [Galactic Civil War](/wiki/Galactic_Civil_War "Galactic Civil War").[[95]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-95) His final apprentice, [Luke Skywalker](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker "Luke Skywalker") endeavored to become a Jedi Knight, but risked a [confrontation](/wiki/Duel_on_Cloud_City "Duel on Cloud City") with Darth Vader—unaware at the time of his family lineage as the Dark Lord's son—before his Jedi training was finished.[[96]](#cite_note-Episode_V-96) Skywalker's decision left Kenobi questioning if the young Jedi apprentice was their last hope and heard the voice of Windu along with other Jedi who fell with the Order in his question.[[94]](#cite_note-There_is_Always_Another-94)

#### Luke Skywalker's judgment

:   "*He remained suspicious of the motives of those in political power, an instinct that proved well-founded when Supreme Chancellor Palpatine was revealed to be the Sith Lord Darth Sidious. Master Windu led a group of Jedi Masters to arrest the corrupt leader, and had my father not betrayed him, he might have bested the Dark Lord in combat.*"
:   ―Luke Skywalker[[97]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Jedi-97)

 [![Mace Windu was remembered as a respected and valiant Jedi Master by Luke Skywalker, the son of Anakin Skywalker.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/15/Luke_Skywalker_Ep_7_SWCT.png/revision/latest?cb=20180731193551) [![Mace Windu was remembered as a respected and valiant Jedi Master by Luke Skywalker, the son of Anakin Skywalker.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/15/Luke_Skywalker_Ep_7_SWCT.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20180731193551)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/15/Luke_Skywalker_Ep_7_SWCT.png/revision/latest?cb=20180731193551) 

Mace Windu was remembered as a respected and valiant Jedi Master by Luke Skywalker, the son of Anakin Skywalker.

 

With the fall of the Empire and the [rise](/wiki/New_Republic_Era "New Republic Era") of the [New Republic](/wiki/New_Republic "New Republic"), an effort to restore the Jedi Order was undertaken by Luke Skywalker, whose research uncovered much of the Order's history along with the lives of notable Jedi Masters such as Windu. Skywalker learned of Windu's reputation as a respected Jedi Master who served in the ranks of the Jedi High Council during the Order's final years. He also learned about Windu's strong commitment to the Order as well as his military service to the Galactic Republic during the Clone Wars.[[97]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Jedi-97)

Skywalker regarded Windu with high esteem because of his adherence to Jedi doctrine, referring to him as a true defender of the Jedi Order's principles. In his [book](/wiki/Book "Book"), *[The Secrets of the Jedi](/wiki/The_Secrets_of_the_Jedi "The Secrets of the Jedi")*, Skywalker acknowledged Windu as a valiant general who fought for the Grand Army of the Republic. He was also aware that Windu was distrustful of politicians and therefore concerned by the Order's entangled relationship with the Galactic Senate. Skywalker believed that Windu's suspicious nature was ultimately vindicated by Darth Sidious' rise to power as Supreme Chancellor Palpatine. He learned that Windu had led a group of Jedi Masters to arrest Sidious, and that Anakin Skywalker intervened by aiding the chancellor. Luke regarded Sidious as corrupt and Anakin's interference as an act of betrayal. Skywalker believed that Windu could have defeated the Dark Lord of the Sith if his father had not turned against the Jedi.[[97]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Jedi-97)

#### Communion with Rey

:   "*Feel the Force flowing through you, Rey.*"
:   ―Mace Windu, to Rey[[98]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-98)

In [35 ABY](/wiki/35_ABY "35 ABY"),[[3]](#cite_note-Timelines-3) during the [Battle of Exegol](/wiki/Battle_of_Exegol "Battle of Exegol"), Windu's voice was heard by [Rey](/wiki/Rey_Skywalker "Rey Skywalker") among the voices of other legendary Jedi of the past. With their help and the help of Anakin Skywalker's grandson, [Ben Solo](/wiki/Ben_Solo "Ben Solo"), Rey destroyed her [grandfather](/wiki/Palpatine_family "Palpatine family"), the resurrected Darth Sidious.[[99]](#cite_note-TSWB-99) She succeeded in this by using [Leia Organa's lightsaber](/wiki/Leia%27s_lightsaber "Leia's lightsaber") and [Luke Skywalker's lightsaber](/wiki/Skywalker_lightsaber "Skywalker lightsaber") to reflect Sidious' Force lightning upon him, disintegrating the Emperor's cloned body.[[98]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-98)

## Personality and traits

### Physical appearance

Mace Windu was a [human](/wiki/Human "Human")[[5]](#cite_note-SWE-5) [male](/wiki/Gender "Gender")[[4]](#cite_note-Databank-4) who had brown [eyes](/wiki/Eye "Eye"), dark skin,[[9]](#cite_note-TPM-9) a strong build, and a height of 1.92 [meters](/wiki/Meter "Meter").[[4]](#cite_note-Databank-4) His head was completely bald; although in his youth, Windu had black [hair](/wiki/Hair "Hair") and a [braid](/wiki/Padawan_braid "Padawan braid") that marked his status as a Padawan.[[6]](#cite_note-JoRMW4-6)

### Youth

:   "*You would twist such a beautiful thing as* faith *into something so vile. Wring out what measly credits and adoration you could from these poor people—all while besmirching the esteem of the Jedi Order. And you think that punishment would not find its way to your doorstep? Yet you claim* we *are the stupid ones… I will make sure you* never *hurt another soul again. This I vow… As a* true *Jedi.*"
:   ―Mace Windu, to Drooz[[6]](#cite_note-JoRMW4-6)

 [![Windu devoted his life to the Jedi Order, but struggled in his youth to temper his emotions.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/00/MaceDrooz-JOTRMaceWindu4.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190118021228) [![Windu devoted his life to the Jedi Order, but struggled in his youth to temper his emotions.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/00/MaceDrooz-JOTRMaceWindu4.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/223?cb=20190118021228)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/00/MaceDrooz-JOTRMaceWindu4.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190118021228) 

Windu devoted his life to the Jedi Order, but struggled in his youth to temper his emotions.

 

Mace Windu was devoted to the Jedi Order ever since his formative years as a Padawan learner. However, in his youth he struggled to temper the frustrations he harbored over the things that offended the ideals of the Jedi, which Windu held as sacred. While his feelings were not inherently wrong according to his mentor, Jedi Master Cyslin Myr, she nonetheless believed that her apprentice needed to convert his hostility into a positive force. During their mission on Mathas, he regarded Drooz's use of religion as offensive, having noticed how the false prophet took advantage of his followers' faith. Faith was a beautiful concept to a spiritual young man like Windu, and as such he could not tolerate the heretical actions of Drooz.[[6]](#cite_note-JoRMW4-6)

Windu, even as a youngling, never responded well to Yoda's humor, which became a reason the Grand Master kept making his jokes, enabling him to often tease the younger Jedi.[[17]](#cite_note-Queen's_Peril-17) Although he struggled to temper his animosity for heretics and con artists, Windu expressed empathy for other people, in particular the natives of Mathas who suffered from the effects of the Niffin plague. He saw them as innocents, but was also stunned by their refusal to see Drooz as a charlatan instead of a prophet. While in pursuit of Drooz, who mocked Windu by insulting the esteem of the Jedi Order, the young Jedi almost took Drooz's life, believing he deserved to be punished for using the Jedi's own belief system to prey on the people who expressed faith in the Force.[[6]](#cite_note-JoRMW4-6)

### Jedi Master

:   "*Doubt* not *the ways of the Force. It tests us at times, but believe it will lead us where we are meant to be, we must. Similarly, doubt not* yourself*. You are a* wise *and* capable *leader.*"
:   ―Yoda, to Mace Windu[[10]](#cite_note-JoRMW1-10)

 [![Grand Master Yoda, the oldest and wisest member of the Jedi Order, held Windu in high esteem.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7c/Masters_of_the_Order.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150926110104) [![Grand Master Yoda, the oldest and wisest member of the Jedi Order, held Windu in high esteem.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7c/Masters_of_the_Order.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/233?cb=20150926110104)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7c/Masters_of_the_Order.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150926110104) 

Grand Master Yoda, the oldest and wisest member of the Jedi Order, held Windu in high esteem.

 

As a Jedi Master, Mace Windu was both disciplined and steadfast, as well as unwaveringly committed to the doctrine of the Jedi Order.[[99]](#cite_note-TSWB-99) A clever[[17]](#cite_note-Queen's_Peril-17) and senior member of the High Council, Windu sought to protect the Order from the corruption and unrest within the Galactic Republic. Although he firmly believed in the Jedi's role as servants of the Republic, the relationship between the Order and the Senate made him uncomfortable.[[97]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Jedi-97) Noted for his grim demeanor, Windu held corrupt politicians and rebellious Jedi in low regard. He had very little patience for the failures of the Senate and was disdainful of Jedi who disobeyed the will of the High Council.[[4]](#cite_note-Databank-4) Obi-Wan Kenobi found that Windu had a habit of scowling at everyone.[[94]](#cite_note-There_is_Always_Another-94) Holding the Jedi teachings as sacrosanct, Windu was suspicious of anyone he perceived to be a threat to the traditions of the Order.[[99]](#cite_note-TSWB-99) He often debated the "maverick" Jedi Qui-Gon Jinn, but neither of them enjoyed such discussions.[[17]](#cite_note-Queen's_Peril-17)

A staunch traditionalist in many ways,[[19]](#cite_note-Knights_Fate-19) Windu was long regarded as the great champion of the Jedi Order. His commitment to the Order's ancient traditions often put him at odds with less orthodox Jedi, such as Qui-Gon Jinn and especially Anakin Skywalker.[[4]](#cite_note-Databank-4) All the same, Windu's reputation as a traditionalist was somewhat challenged by the fact he created the Vaapad form of lightsaber combat, doing so out of a recognition that an internal darkness existed within himself; through Vaapad, he reasoned, he could channel that darkness to positive ends.[[19]](#cite_note-Knights_Fate-19) In the days before the Naboo Crisis, when he thought Yoda was hiding something, he went straight to talk to the Grand Master, who waited for Windu to "crack" by not speaking. During their discussion, the two found they disagreed on whether "something" and "nothing" were opposites; Windu, feeling they were indeed opposites, was sure of himself, while Yoda did not like to presume the unknown. Windu also did not enjoy the exposure that came when one of his questions was turned back at him. Despite finding Yoda's behaviors distracting, he always respected Yoda's judgement and knew to follow his training, deciding the Force would educate him about the issue when the time came.[[17]](#cite_note-Queen's_Peril-17)

 [![Mace Windu wields his purple lightsaber.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/71/MaceWindu-TLC.png/revision/latest?cb=20230613022332) [![Mace Windu wields his purple lightsaber.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/71/MaceWindu-TLC.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20230613022332)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/71/MaceWindu-TLC.png/revision/latest?cb=20230613022332) 

Mace Windu wields his purple lightsaber.

 

In their first encounter, Windu was unimpressed with Skywalker.[[28]](#cite_note-USW-28) He was not only skeptical of Skywalker's status as the Chosen One, but also felt that he was too old to dedicate himself to the ways of the Jedi.[[99]](#cite_note-TSWB-99) Despite his reservations however, Windu came to respect Skywalker even as early as his first days as a Padawan[[8]](#cite_note-Glass_Abyss-8) and came to regard Skywalker as an exceptionally skilled, yet tempestuous Jedi. They had a cordial relationship during the Clone Wars and bantered with each other on a first-name basis when working together.[[60]](#cite_note-Death_Trap-60)

While he respected Skywalker's skills, he still saw the young Jedi Knight as too emotional. As such by the end of the Clone Wars, Windu began having doubts that Skywalker was the Chosen One destined to bring balance to the Force. He had grave doubts about Skywalker's appointment to the High Council at the insistence of Chancellor Palpatine,[[99]](#cite_note-TSWB-99) and believed it was too dangerous to have Skywalker spy on Palpatine.[[33]](#cite_note-ROTS-33) Kenobi sometimes felt Windu had a special frown reserved just for Skywalker.[[94]](#cite_note-There_is_Always_Another-94)

Windu's reservations were overshadowed by the start of the Clone Wars.[[99]](#cite_note-TSWB-99) In the early days of the conflict, Windu wrestled with feelings of uncertainty concerning the Jedi's new role as warriors, as well as remorse for the Jedi who died during the Battle of Geonosis. In his moments of doubt, he turned to Yoda seeking wisdom and guidance. The ancient Grand Master advised his fellow Councilor to keep faith in the will of the Force; nor question his role in the Order, for in Yoda's eyes, Windu was a wise and capable leader. During a mission on Hissrich, Windu's faith was further tested by his interactions with the Jedi Prosset Dibs, who harbored his own reservations about the Order's part in the conflict.[[10]](#cite_note-JoRMW1-10)

 [![As a member of the High Council, Windu was determined to protect the traditions and independence of the Jedi Order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/44/Councilrots.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090915231817) [![As a member of the High Council, Windu was determined to protect the traditions and independence of the Jedi Order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/44/Councilrots.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/271?cb=20090915231817)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/44/Councilrots.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090915231817) 

As a member of the High Council, Windu was determined to protect the traditions and independence of the Jedi Order.

 

Whereas Dibs grew increasingly doubtful, believing the Jedi did not belong on the battlefield, Windu became more certain that—as Jedi Knights—they had a duty to protect the innocent and restore peace to the galaxy. Dibs ultimately accused the Jedi Order of turning away from their traditions, causing Windu to hold fast to his conviction that it was not wrong to fight for the ideals he believed in. The Jedi, Windu felt, never wanted to fight in a war,[[6]](#cite_note-JoRMW4-6) but circumstances compelled them to become a sword instead of a shield for the Republic.[[10]](#cite_note-JoRMW1-10)

Windu held Skywalker's apprentice, Padawan Ahsoka Tano, as another rebellious Jedi.[[4]](#cite_note-Databank-4) When Tano was framed for treason, Windu supported the High Council's decision to revoke her status as a Jedi and turn her over to the Republic for a military tribunal.[[67]](#cite_note-The_Wrong_Jedi-67) While their verdict pained him,[[72]](#cite_note-Episode_Gallery-72) Windu concurred with Tarkin's position on the matter—an internal Jedi trial would appear biased, and to protect Tano would be to defy the wishes of the Senate. He therefore felt that submitting Tano for trial was the only feasible option available to the Council. After her innocence was proven, however, Windu joined his colleagues in offering to welcome Tano back into the Order, and proclaimed her a greater Jedi because of her ordeal, which he observed as the great trial in her path to Jedi Knighthood. Tano refused to come back, a decision which surprised Windu and the Council.[[67]](#cite_note-The_Wrong_Jedi-67)

 [![Until the Clone Wars forced him to adapt, Mace Windu was committed to the ancient ways of the Jedi Order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b1/GlassAbyss-cropped.png/revision/latest?cb=20240626034709) [![Until the Clone Wars forced him to adapt, Mace Windu was committed to the ancient ways of the Jedi Order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b1/GlassAbyss-cropped.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20240626034709)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b1/GlassAbyss-cropped.png/revision/latest?cb=20240626034709) 

Until the Clone Wars forced him to adapt, Mace Windu was committed to the ancient ways of the Jedi Order.

 

Notwithstanding his commitment to the ancient traditions of the Order, the Clone Wars forced Windu to rethink some of his beliefs and preconceptions,[[4]](#cite_note-Databank-4) pushing his fellow Jedi to take actions that were previously considered unthinkable.[[100]](#cite_note-Join_the_Battle-100) He held fast to the Order's rigid code throughout the Clone Wars, but also began to consider its potential shortcomings.[[99]](#cite_note-TSWB-99) Prior to the Battle of Geonosis, Windu did not believe it was in the nature of a Jedi—even a former one such as Count Dooku—to assassinate anyone. The onset of the Clone Wars caused Windu to realize that his old friend was more than a "political idealist"; Dooku had joined the dark side as an enemy of the Order and the Republic he had once served.[[7]](#cite_note-AOTC-7) As the death toll escalated after nearly three years of continuous warfare, Windu proposed to have Dooku assassinated in the hope of preventing further civilian casualties. Although his colleague, Obi-Wan Kenobi, asserted that assassination was against the Jedi Code, Windu pointed out that it was also against the Jedi way to allow innocent people to suffer needlessly.[[79]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-79)

### Diplomat and general

:   "*This respected member of the Jedi High Council and general in the Clone Wars was a true defender of the Jedi Order and all that it stood for. Although he fought valiantly for the Grand Army of the Republic, Master Windu was never comfortable with how the Jedi and the Senate had become so deeply intertwined.*"
:   ―Luke Skywalker[[97]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Jedi-97)

 [![Windu was a respected negotiator and diplomat.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c4/MaceWindu-TSSOCE.png/revision/latest?cb=20230318043129) [![Windu was a respected negotiator and diplomat.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c4/MaceWindu-TSSOCE.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230318043129)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c4/MaceWindu-TSSOCE.png/revision/latest?cb=20230318043129) 

Windu was a respected negotiator and diplomat.

 

As the war progressed, Windu was compelled to engage in politics. Although he disliked the system, he nonetheless proved to be an able diplomat during the Ryloth campaign in which he successfully mediated a truce between two rivals, Senator Orn Free Taa and Cham Syndulla.[[4]](#cite_note-Databank-4) His efforts to find a diplomatic solution were less successful on Anaxes, however. Upon confronting a regiment of battle droids, he offered to have them reprogrammed in return for their unconditional surrender, citing his capacity for destroying Separatist droids as a reason to avoid fighting him. Their response was to attack, forcing Windu and Kenobi to defend themselves.[[82]](#cite_note-Unfinished_Business-82) He also cared for the lives of his soldiers, such as when used the Force to make sure two clones did not die, even though he was in danger himself during the deed.[[46]](#cite_note-Liberty_on_Ryloth-46)

In spite of how the conflict forced the Jedi into the role of generals and warriors, Windu held fast to the Jedi Code, considering moral foundations to be vital. When the Dugs of Malastare proposed to kill the Zillo Beast, Windu refused to support them and presumed that the beast was the last of its kind.[[4]](#cite_note-Databank-4) He also chose to not seek retribution against Boba Fett after the latter attempted to assassinate him.[[61]](#cite_note-Lethal_Trackdown-61) Despite his disapproval of maverick Jedi and the avarice of the Senate, Windu was very loyal to both the Republic and the Jedi Order to the point where he bravely risked his life for both institutions throughout the Clone Wars.[[4]](#cite_note-Databank-4) Even as the Jedi became officers in the Grand Army of the Republic,[[7]](#cite_note-AOTC-7) Windu remained extremely protective of the Order's independence and jealously guarded its interests against external interference.[[33]](#cite_note-ROTS-33)

### Jedi Champion

:   "*We do what we have trained our whole lives to do. Trust in the Force. Believe in the path that is set out before us. Stand in defense of all peoples, not just of the Republic, but across the galaxy. We do what any Jedi would when staring into the face of evil. We fight.*"
:   ―Mace Windu, to Rissa Mano[[40]](#cite_note-JoRMW5-40)

 [![Mace Windu was known as the great champion of the Jedi Order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4a/Windu_Angry.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20091201175459) [![Mace Windu was known as the great champion of the Jedi Order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4a/Windu_Angry.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20091201175459)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4a/Windu_Angry.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20091201175459) 

Mace Windu was known as the great champion of the Jedi Order.

 

Though noted for his grim demeanor,[[4]](#cite_note-Databank-4) Windu was highly compassionate towards his fellow Jedi, the citizens of the Republic,[[79]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-79) and the clone troopers under his command.[[60]](#cite_note-Death_Trap-60) His own survival on Geonosis was of little comfort to him; the galaxy had fallen into a state of war, and the Jedi—once the peacekeepers of the Republic—were forced to adopt the mantle of warriors and military leaders. Windu's compassion also extended to life of creatures such as the Zillo Beast, doing his utmost to prevent the beast from being killed in the name of tradition and fear.[[4]](#cite_note-Databank-4)

Windu worked closely with Supreme Chancellor Sheev Palpatine, often acting as an adviser to the leader of the Senate throughout the Clone Wars.[[41]](#cite_note-TCW-film-41) As time went on, the Jedi champion grew increasingly suspicious of Palpatine's intentions. During the Zillo Beast's transportation to Coruscant, Windu strongly disagreed with the chancellor's decision to bring the dangerous creature to the Republic capital.[[4]](#cite_note-Databank-4) Though wary of Palpatine, Windu remained committed to his duty as a Jedi, which required him to ensure the safety of the chancellor. Yet even this responsibility resulted in a disagreement between himself and the chancellor; Palpatine claimed that the level of security around him was unnecessary during his visit to Naboo, but Windu insisted on taking every precaution to protect the chancellor.[[66]](#cite_note-Crisis_on_Naboo-66)

 [![Windu confronted Sidious in the hope of preventing the Jedi Order's destruction.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3b/Vaapad.png/revision/latest?cb=20130210043146) [![Windu confronted Sidious in the hope of preventing the Jedi Order's destruction.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3b/Vaapad.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130210043146)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3b/Vaapad.png/revision/latest?cb=20130210043146) 

Windu confronted Sidious in the hope of preventing the Jedi Order's destruction.

 

In the waning days of the Clone Wars, Windu's trust and respect for Palpatine had all but evaporated. Following Dooku's death, he was uncertain whether Palpatine would relinquish his wartime authority as he once promised. At the same time, Windu came to sense the dark side of the Force surrounding the chancellor. By now he was certain that a plot was in motion to destroy the Jedi Order. When Skywalker confirmed that Palpatine's true identity was Darth Sidious, Windu was determined to take swift and decisive action against the Sith Lord, realizing that the fate of the Jedi Order hung in the balance. Although he initially attempted to arrest Sidious, Windu concluded that it was impossible to seek justice due to the chancellor's hold over the system. He therefore decided to end Sidious' life before the latter could succeed in his plan to fully take over the Republic, despite Skywalker's insistence that killing the Sith Lord—disarmed and seemingly beaten—was against the Jedi Code. However, in concentrating all of his attention on preventing the galaxy from falling under Sith oppression, Windu failed to anticipate Skywalker's intervention, resulting in the demise of the Jedi Order's great champion.[[4]](#cite_note-Databank-4)

## Powers and abilities

Windu was a highly-regarded Jedi Master whose exploits within the battlefield during the Clone Wars, prowess as a warrior, and history within the as a Jedi made him both universally regarded and a champion of the Jedi Order.[[4]](#cite_note-Databank-4) Within the Jedi Order, he was considered second to Jedi Grand Master Yoda in reputation.[[28]](#cite_note-USW-28)

### Lightsaber abilities

:   "*I have studied his teachings since I was a youngling. His style of lightsaber combat has been the foundation of my own. He is a top five Jedi Master of all time* for sure*!*"
:   ―Rissa Mano, on Mace Windu[[10]](#cite_note-JoRMW1-10)

 [![Mace Windu was a master in lightsaber combat.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b6/Shatterpoint-Winduwallpaper.png/revision/latest?cb=20231119230125) [![Mace Windu was a master in lightsaber combat.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b6/Shatterpoint-Winduwallpaper.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20231119230125)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b6/Shatterpoint-Winduwallpaper.png/revision/latest?cb=20231119230125) 

Mace Windu was a master in lightsaber combat.

 

Having studied under Cyslin Myr as her apprentice, as well as learning under Yoda[[101]](#cite_note-Jedi_Pocket_Expert-101) and T'ra Saa,[[8]](#cite_note-Glass_Abyss-8) Windu was a highly-accomplished lightsaber duelist considered to be among the best ever produced by the Jedi Order,[[28]](#cite_note-USW-28) a opinion shared by even enemies such as the Sith Lord Darth Sidious.[[13]](#cite_note-Brotherhood-13)

Most notably, he was a one of the two masters (other being [Depa Billaba](/wiki/Depa_Billaba "Depa Billaba")) of both variants of [Form VII](/wiki/Form_VII "Form VII"),[[102]](#cite_note-ECUC-102) having created the Vaapad variant in as a mean to address and to control his inner darkness and channel it towards productive means while making it in line with the Jedi Code. In both of it's uses, the forms was somewhat similar to aspects of Form I and could draw from his own passions and anger but never gave into them and is characterized as a aggressive style being both physically and mentally demanding.[[19]](#cite_note-Knights_Fate-19) These combat techniques often treaded closely to dark side practices[[28]](#cite_note-USW-28) but was a unique fighting style that made him a superior combatant and capable of defeating multiple opponents.[[99]](#cite_note-TSWB-99) Throughout his lifetime, he displayed his formidable skills against capable opponents, including fellow Jedi Master [Prosset Dibs](/wiki/Tenth_Brother "Tenth Brother"),[[6]](#cite_note-JoRMW4-6) Mother [Talzin](/wiki/Talzin "Talzin") of the [Nightsisters](/wiki/Nightsisters "Nightsisters"),[[73]](#cite_note-Disappeared_2-73) [Dooku](/wiki/Dooku "Dooku") after his conversion as a Sith Lord[[58]](#cite_note-SAP2-58), and Darth Sidious whose skills dispatched 3 other fellow Jedi Masters. Windu not only was the sole survivor of the initial assault but ultimately gained the upper hand, disarmed, and nearly prevailed in killing the Sith Lord.[[4]](#cite_note-Databank-4) Luke Skywalker opined that without Skywalker's intervention, he would have killed the Sith Lord.[[97]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Jedi-97)

Windu was also highly adept at deflecting incoming blaster shots with his lightsaber. During the Battle of Geonosis, Windu charged towards Jango Fett while simultaneously deflecting his fire before ultimately disarming and decapitating the bounty hunter in a swift motion. Afterward, he continued to utilize his skills at blaster deflection against an overwhelming number of battle droids, which enabled him to survive long enough until Yoda and the clone army arrived and turned the tide of the battle in the Republic's favor.[[4]](#cite_note-Databank-4) Throughout the Clone Wars, Windu continued to rely on this defensive technique when leading Republic forces on the frontlines, especially during the Ryloth campaign.[[46]](#cite_note-Liberty_on_Ryloth-46) In addition to blaster shots, Windu could use his lightsaber to block a Force lightning attack, which he could also redirect back to its source in a superconducting loop.[[33]](#cite_note-ROTS-33)

### Force powers

:   "*Sending a call to other Jedi through the Force was the* second *lesson I learned as a Padawan…*"
:   ―Mace Windu[[14]](#cite_note-Age_of_Republic-14)

 [![Mace Windu was skilled in the Force, including the power of telekinesis.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/SW_JotR_Mace_Windu_1-cover.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180312123608) [![Mace Windu was skilled in the Force, including the power of telekinesis.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/SW_JotR_Mace_Windu_1-cover.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20180312123608)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/SW_JotR_Mace_Windu_1-cover.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180312123608) 

Mace Windu was skilled in the Force, including the power of telekinesis.

 

Alongside his formidable abilities with a lightsaber, Windu was also considered nearly unmatched with his powers within the Force.[[103]](#cite_note-Star_Wars:_Galactic_Atlas-103) Darth Sidious also considered Windu to possibly to be the most powerful Force adept in the Jedi Order during the early days of the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars").[[13]](#cite_note-Brotherhood-13)

As a Force adept, his abilities included Force-enhanced reflexes and agility, the ability to see the future,[[99]](#cite_note-TSWB-99) and possessed enhanced senses[[33]](#cite_note-ROTS-33) although certain aspects of his abilities (seeing the future and his senses) were partially diminished due to the dark side having clouded him alongside the order, disallowing him to see the future at will during his years as the elected Master of the Order.[[104]](#cite_note-The_Living_Force-104) By the ending days of the Clone Wars, he was able to sense that the dark side of the Force clustered around Palpatine and a plot to destroy the Jedi Order but could not discover the Chancellor's dual identity as a Sith Lord.[[33]](#cite_note-ROTS-33) Windu was also skilled in more rare Force abilities such as [battle meditation](/wiki/Battle_meditation "Battle meditation") and was able to sense [shatterpoints](/wiki/Shatterpoint "Shatterpoint"), key moments where actions could change eventually.[[100]](#cite_note-Join_the_Battle-100)

Windu was proficient in various forms of [telekinesis](/wiki/Telekinesis "Telekinesis"), which he could utilize as both attacks and defenses. He was capable of easily summoning his lightsaber, as demonstrated on Geonosis when he quickly reclaimed his Jedi weapon by way of the Force before Fett could prevent this.[[7]](#cite_note-AOTC-7) On Ryloth he used the Force to telekinetically pull battle droids in his direction, rendering them vulnerable to a fatal lightsaber attack. He was also powerful enough to levitate individuals, such as two clone troopers whose lives he saved by using the Force to prevent them from falling to their deaths. In addition to the offensive and defensive applications of the Force, Windu could use his connection to the Force to enhance his physical capabilities, allowing him to engage in acrobatics and land [jumps](/wiki/Force_jump "Force jump") from high places without sustaining injuries.[[46]](#cite_note-Liberty_on_Ryloth-46) He could use the Force to greatly [enhance his speed](/wiki/Force_Dash "Force Dash"), notably against battle droids.[[10]](#cite_note-JoRMW1-10)

Windu's abilities with the Force extended to mind control, a Jedi technique that allowed the user to exert a considerable amount of influence over weak-minded individuals. Against a person of greater willpower than the average being, however, Windu was forced to combine his effort with Skywalker and Kenobi in order to force Cad Bane's cooperation. Although the initial attempt failed, their combined use of the "mind trick" technique caused Bane to experience significant discomfort, which nearly damaged his mind in the process.[[51]](#cite_note-Children_of_the_Force-51) Additionally, Windu had the ability to communicate with other Jedi through the Force, making it easier for them to find his location.[[14]](#cite_note-Age_of_Republic-14)

### Other skills

Windu was well-versed in both armed and [unarmed combat](/wiki/Unarmed_combat "Unarmed combat"); He was able to incapacitate multiple [Gamorreans](/wiki/Gamorrean "Gamorrean") in his youth unarmed[[6]](#cite_note-JoRMW4-6) and fended off two [gundarks](/wiki/Gundark "Gundark") on his own for a time when deprived of his lightsaber with both unarmed skills and strength.[[73]](#cite_note-Disappeared_2-73) He was a practitioner of [Na Jang](/wiki/Na_Jang "Na Jang").[[8]](#cite_note-Glass_Abyss-8) He was also versed in utilizing different weaponry such as a [spear](/wiki/Spear "Spear")[[74]](#cite_note-Disappeared_1-74) and a [baton](/wiki/Baton "Baton"), sometimes using these skills to not draw attention as a Jedi.[[20]](#cite_note-Windu1-20) During his years as a Jedi Knight, Windu often undertook special missions and possessed a versatile skillset, having been a apt [slicer](/wiki/Slicer "Slicer"), starfighter pilot, could infiltrate highly security facilities and go undercover.[[20]](#cite_note-Windu1-20)[[18]](#cite_note-Rev23-18) He was also a skilled actor and was taught to perform Rodian theater works of Harido Kavila by [Alxa Kress](/wiki/Alxa_Kress "Alxa Kress"), making him also fluent in [Rodese](/wiki/Rodian_(language) "Rodian (language)"). These skills also could enable him to adopt convincing disguises able to fool fellow Jedi.[[35]](#cite_note-Choose_Your_Destiny-35)

Although he held a personal disdain for politics and was uncomfortable within a military role,[[97]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Jedi-97) Windu proved to be both a capable diplomat[[4]](#cite_note-Databank-4) and was a highly-regarded warrior of the Grand Army of the Republic who was considered an elite military officer[[28]](#cite_note-USW-28) and the Jedi High Council's top battlefield general.[[105]](#cite_note-AEYNK-105)

## Equipment

### Clothing

Mace Windu wore [Jedi apparel](/wiki/Jedi_apparel "Jedi apparel") that included a brown [cloak](/wiki/Cloak "Cloak") with wide sleeves and a deep hood along with a undertunic, and a tan overtunic.[[7]](#cite_note-AOTC-7) His outfit also included a [belt](/wiki/Belt "Belt") and pouches for common Jedi gear such as a [comlink](/wiki/Comlink "Comlink"), [grappling hooks](/wiki/Grappling_hook "Grappling hook"), [holoprojector](/wiki/Holoprojector "Holoprojector"), and a [rebreather](/wiki/Rebreather "Rebreather").[[97]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Jedi-97)[[20]](#cite_note-Windu1-20) During the Clone Wars, he instead wore a long-sleeved tanned undertunic with [plastoid](/wiki/Plastoid "Plastoid") gauntlets with the Jedi Order insignia on it.[[47]](#cite_note-Supply_lines-47) As a Jedi Knight, when he performed assignments on more arctic or cold worlds, he owned a white coat and goggles.[[20]](#cite_note-Windu1-20)

### Lightsaber

 [![Mace Windu's lightsaber emitted an amethyst-colored blade.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2d/Windu_Lightsaber_DB.png/revision/latest?cb=20221116044314) [![Mace Windu's lightsaber emitted an amethyst-colored blade.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2d/Windu_Lightsaber_DB.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/181?cb=20221116044314)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2d/Windu_Lightsaber_DB.png/revision/latest?cb=20221116044314) 

Mace Windu's lightsaber emitted an amethyst-colored blade.

 

During his lifetime as a Jedi, Windu had built at least two lightsabers, both in which produced a purple-hued lightsaber; his second lightsaber was crafted with the highest standards of precision, creating a superior weapon that reflected on his mature abilities as a figure of leadership within the Jedi Order.[[28]](#cite_note-USW-28) The hilt of his lightsaber was polished in electrum and had golden highlights, indicating his status as a senior member of the Jedi High Council.[[106]](#cite_note-The_Lightsaber_Collection-106) The amethyst-colored blade served as warning to adversaries that the Jedi Order's greatest champion was ready to battle.[[27]](#cite_note-Windu's_Lightsaber-27)

## Behind the scenes

:   "*We were so lucky that Samuel was willing to play the role again. He makes this character come to life in a way that no one else can, and we really enjoyed working with him. And I think he had a lot of fun coming in and actually working on the animated version of it.*"
:   ―[Catherine Winder](/wiki/Catherine_Winder "Catherine Winder"), on the DVD audio commentary for *The Clone Wars* film[[107]](#cite_note-TCW_film_commentary-107)

 [![Mace Windu was played by Samuel L. Jackson, who requested a purple lightsaber from George Lucas.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/38/Samuel_L_Jackson_at_San_Diego_ComicCon_2008.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120612164437) [![Mace Windu was played by Samuel L. Jackson, who requested a purple lightsaber from George Lucas.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/38/Samuel_L_Jackson_at_San_Diego_ComicCon_2008.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120612164437)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/38/Samuel_L_Jackson_at_San_Diego_ComicCon_2008.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120612164437) 

Mace Windu was played by Samuel L. Jackson, who requested a purple lightsaber from George Lucas.

 

[Samuel L. Jackson](/wiki/Samuel_L._Jackson "Samuel L. Jackson") portrayed Mace Windu in the [prequel trilogy](/wiki/Prequel_trilogy "Prequel trilogy") and he returned to voice the character in the [*Star Wars: The Clone Wars* film](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Clone_Wars_(film) "Star Wars: The Clone Wars (film)").[[107]](#cite_note-TCW_film_commentary-107) In the *[Star Wars: The Clone Wars](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Clone_Wars "Star Wars: The Clone Wars")* TV series, his voice was provided by [Terrence Carson](/wiki/Terrence_Carson "Terrence Carson"), who had also played the role in various [Legends](/wiki/Star_Wars_Legends "Star Wars Legends") animation and video games. Windu is also voiced by Carson in *[Star Wars: Tales of the Jedi](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Tales_of_the_Jedi_(television_series) "Star Wars: Tales of the Jedi (television series)")* and some non-canon media. He is the official "audio double" for the character.[[25]](#cite_note-TOTJ-Choices-25) Jackson reenacted scenes with the character in a March 2017 episode of [*The Late Late Show with James Corden*](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Late_Late_Show_with_James_Corden "wikipedia:The Late Late Show with James Corden").[[108]](#cite_note-James_Corden-108)

The name "Mace Windu" was already featured in the earliest incarnation of what would become *[Star Wars](/wiki/Star_Wars "Star Wars")*—a 13-page document written by [George Lucas](/wiki/George_Lucas "George Lucas") in [1973](/wiki/1973 "1973"). According to Concept Artist [Iain McCaig](/wiki/Iain_McCaig "Iain McCaig"), early artwork of Windu was based on the face of [Industrial Light & Magic](/wiki/Industrial_Light_%26_Magic "Industrial Light & Magic") modeler Steve Aplin, before the casting of Samuel L. Jackson.[[109]](#cite_note-old-db-bts-109)

Jackson requested George Lucas that his character be given a purple lightsaber because he wanted to be able to find himself in the [Geonosis battle scene](/wiki/First_Battle_of_Geonosis "First Battle of Geonosis") in [*Attack of the Clones*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_II_Attack_of_the_Clones "Star Wars: Episode II Attack of the Clones"). He reasoned that, since Windu is the second most powerful Jedi after Yoda, Windu should have a lightsaber of a different color from the customary red, blue, and green. As a reference for Jackson's iconic role in the film *Pulp Fiction* the crew presented him with a lightsaber "BMF" engraved on the hilt, standing for the phrase "*bad motherfucker*".[[110]](#cite_note-Graham_Norton_Show-110)

Following [Lucasfilm](/wiki/Lucasfilm "Lucasfilm")'s buyout by [The Walt Disney Company](/wiki/The_Walt_Disney_Company "The Walt Disney Company") in [2012](/wiki/2012 "2012") and the announcement of the *Star Wars* [sequel trilogy](/wiki/Sequel_trilogy "Sequel trilogy"), Jackson expressed interest in reprising his role in the [2015](/wiki/2015 "2015") film [*Star Wars*: Episode VII *The Force Awakens*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_VII_The_Force_Awakens "Star Wars: Episode VII The Force Awakens"), opining that he could return as a [Force spirit](/wiki/Force_spirit "Force spirit") given Windu's death in *Revenge of the Sith*.[[111]](#cite_note-Windu_VII-111) The actor further expressed his interest in playing Windu again in the *[Star Wars Anthology Series](/wiki/Star_Wars_Anthology_Series "Star Wars Anthology Series")*, insisting that character may have survived.[[112]](#cite_note-Windu_Return-112) Jackson eventually reprised his role in a brief vocal cameo in the [2019](/wiki/2019 "2019") film [*Star Wars*: Episode IX *The Rise of Skywalker*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_IX_The_Rise_of_Skywalker "Star Wars: Episode IX The Rise of Skywalker"), the final film of the [Skywalker saga](/wiki/Star_Wars_saga "Star Wars saga").[[98]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-98)

[↑](#cite_ref-Master_&_Apprentice_24-0) *[Master & Apprentice](/wiki/Master_%26_Apprentice "Master & Apprentice")* 25. ↑ [25.0](#cite_ref-TOTJ-Choices_25-0) [25.1](#cite_ref-TOTJ-Choices_25-1) [25.2](#cite_ref-TOTJ-Choices_25-2) [25.3](#cite_ref-TOTJ-Choices_25-3) [25.4](#cite_ref-TOTJ-Choices_25-4) [25.5](#cite_ref-TOTJ-Choices_25-5) [Tales of the Jedi logo](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Tales_of_the_Jedi_(television_series) "Star Wars: Tales of the Jedi (television series)") *[Star Wars: Tales of the Jedi](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Tales_of_the_Jedi_(television_series) "Star Wars: Tales of the Jedi (television series)")* — "[Choices](/wiki/Choices "Choices")" 26. ↑ [26.0](#cite_ref-Choices_date_26-0) [26.1](#cite_ref-Choices_date_26-1) [26.2](#cite_ref-Choices_date_26-2) In "[Choices](/wiki/Choices "Choices")" Mace Windu gains a seat on the [Jedi High Council](/wiki/Jedi_High_Council "Jedi High Council"). [*Star Wars*: Episode III *Revenge of the Sith*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_III_Revenge_of_the_Sith "Star Wars: Episode III Revenge of the Sith") established that [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker") was the youngest to ever serve on the Council. *[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Galactic_Atlas "Star Wars: Galactic Atlas")* dates the film to [19 BBY](/wiki/19_BBY "19 BBY"), while *[Star Wars: On the Front Lines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_On_the_Front_Lines "Star Wars: On the Front Lines")* establishes that Skywalker was born in [41 BBY](/wiki/41_BBY "41 BBY"). Therefore, Windu must have been at least twenty-two years old when he joined the Council. According to the *[Star Wars Encyclopedia](/wiki/Star_Wars_Encyclopedia_(series) "Star Wars Encyclopedia (series)")* booklet "[Mace Windu and Other Users of the Force](/wiki/Mace_Windu_and_Other_Users_of_the_Force "Mace Windu and Other Users of the Force")," Windu was born 40 years before the [Battle of Naboo](/wiki/Battle_of_Naboo "Battle of Naboo"), which *Star Wars: Galactic Atlas* places in [32 BBY](/wiki/32_BBY "32 BBY"). Therefore, Windu gained a seat on the Council not before [50 BBY](/wiki/50_BBY "50 BBY"). The episode takes place before Dooku left the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order"). *[The Star Wars Book](/wiki/The_Star_Wars_Book "The Star Wars Book")* places [Dooku](/wiki/Dooku "Dooku")'s departure from the Jedi Order to forty-two [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") before the events of [*Star Wars*: Episode IV *A New Hope*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_IV_A_New_Hope "Star Wars: Episode IV A New Hope"), which corresponds to [42 BBY](/wiki/42_BBY "42 BBY") according to *Star Wars: Galactic Atlas*. Therefore "Choices" takes place between these years. 27. ↑ [27.0](#cite_ref-Windu's_Lightsaber_27-0) [27.1](#cite_ref-Windu's_Lightsaber_27-1) [27.2](#cite_ref-Windu's_Lightsaber_27-2) [27.3](#cite_ref-Windu's_Lightsaber_27-3) [StarWars-DatabankII](/wiki/Databank_(2014-) "Databank (2014-)") [Mace Windu's Lightsaber](https://www.starwars.com/databank/mace-windus-lightsaber) in the [Databank](/wiki/Databank_(2014-) "Databank (2014-)") ([backup link](https://web.archive.org/web/20190910041626/https://www.starwars.com/databank/mace-windus-lightsaber)) 28. ↑ [28.0](#cite_ref-USW_28-0) [28.1](#cite_ref-USW_28-1) [28.2](#cite_ref-USW_28-2) [28.3](#cite_ref-USW_28-3) [28.4](#cite_ref-USW_28-4) [28.5](#cite_ref-USW_28-5) [28.6](#cite_ref-USW_28-6) *[Ultimate Star Wars](/wiki/Ultimate_Star_Wars "Ultimate Star Wars")* 29. [↑](#cite_ref-Insider_199_29-0) [SWInsider](/wiki/Star_Wars_Insider "Star Wars Insider") "[A Seat on the Council](/wiki/A_Seat_on_the_Council "A Seat on the Council")" — [*Star Wars Insider* 199](/wiki/Star_Wars_Insider_199 "Star Wars Insider 199") 30.
